Domestic Important Telegrams 3

Organization of the Liaoning Finance Department

(Harbin) The General Outline of the Organization of the Liaoning Finance Department, Chapter 1, General Provisions, Article 1: Before the establishment of the new government, the local maintenance committee deems it necessary to revive the Finance Department in order to ensure public order and restore people's livelihoods, and it will determine temporary measures based on its responsibilities in order to achieve its goals. Chapter 2, Article 2: The head of the Finance Department shall be selected by the local maintenance committee. Article 3: The organization and powers of the Finance Department shall temporarily follow the previous system, but must be kept to a minimum. Article 4: In order to handle financial affairs and make them more perfect, the local maintenance committee shall recruit several Japanese advisors for consultation. The head of the Finance Department shall respect the opinions of the advisors regarding the operation of financial administration. Chapter 3, Article 5: The local maintenance committee shall establish a Finance Committee to formulate tax systems, revise budgets, and plan other implementation programs. The scope of the committee shall be as follows: representatives from the Japanese side, representatives from the local maintenance committee, the head of the Finance Department, advisors, section chiefs, representatives from the municipal government, and representatives from the provincial chamber of commerce and agriculture. Supplementary Provisions, Article 6: The head of the Finance Department shall consult with the local maintenance committee and issue the necessary announcements on his own as soon as possible. When implementing them, he must first receive the approval of the Japanese army. Article 7: The local maintenance committee shall formulate temporary measures for the Finance Department, indicating its intention to open the department, and request the approval of the Japanese army and start immediately. Article 8: If any tax officials of the old regime are found to be sending various tax payments, the Japanese army may be requested to severely punish them. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Ma Longtan Relies on Japanese Power to Shamelessly Proclaim Sino-Manchu Independence

Organizing the So-Called Independent Autonomous Association

(Harbin) Ma Longtan, the former supervisor of the Siping-Taonan Railway, is relying on Japanese power in Changtu to organize the Sino-Manchu Independent Autonomous Association, including the four counties of Lishu, Liaoyuan, Huaide, and Kaiyuan. It was established on the 20th and issued an absurd declaration, saying: "Since the Sino-Japanese incident occurred, the Northeast government has been destroyed, the military and police have scattered, rumors have spread, bandits have run rampant, and soldiers have turned into bandits. It is often heard that the people have lost their wealth and homes and are suffering in misery. The chaotic situation is truly unbearable to witness. Now, fortunately, with the cooperation and support of the gentry and people of Changtu, Lishu, Liaoyuan, Huaide, and Kaiyuan counties, the Sino-Manchu Joint Independent Autonomous Association has been established, and all political organs have been re-established. I, Ma Longtan, have received the mandate of heaven and responded to the wishes of the people. I uphold the great mission of the Red Swastika Society and the spirit of love and kindness of all mankind in the world. My highest goal is to build a paradise of Sino-Japanese friendship. Therefore, I declare the Sino-Manchu Joint Independent Autonomous Association, and I hope that people from all walks of life will take note." (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Trends in British and French Newspapers

(London) This morning, the British newspapers all expressed anxiety, fearing that the League of Nations Administrative Council would implement its opinion of abandoning the Manchurian problem. The Liberal Party's Daily News asked Briand and Litvinov to stay in Geneva to save the League of Nations' crisis. The Times' Geneva correspondent made a fair and impartial comment today, saying that if the international community does not use the precedent of 1926 applied to Greece and Bulgaria to put pressure on both sides and send neutral personnel to monitor the situation on the ground to ensure the effectiveness of its pressure, then the Sino-Japanese conflict will have almost no chance of resolution. The League of Nations should assume this responsibility and assist Japan and China in reaching an agreement on the conditions for troop withdrawal. (Reuters Dispatch, 22nd)

(Paris) All newspapers believe that the Administrative Council will be able to conclude everything today. Their opinions on the real achievements of the Administrative Council are very different. Several newspapers seem to fear that the Administrative Council will not be able to reach a positive solution this time. Several other newspapers believe that it would be most convenient for the Administrative Council to extend the meeting for three weeks. However, the date of the reconvening of the Administrative Council must coincide with the date of Japan's complete withdrawal of troops from Manchuria. "Paris Echo" stated that Shi Zhaoji declared again to Briand that China cannot accept any decision that is contrary to the principles contained in the Chinese Memorandum. "Le Petit Parisien" said that if Shi Zhaoji does not completely change his mind, then the Administrative Council will be able to obtain China's consent. In short, whether the Administrative Council obtains complete understanding or only an agreement with conditions that will be further detailed later, its meeting will adjourn or suspend on Saturday. If it is the second result, then the Administrative Council will entrust Briand to monitor the development of the situation and take all the measures proposed by the League of Nations Covenant and the Basic Charter. (Havas Dispatch, 22nd)

Absurd Declaration by Japanese Minister of Finance Inoue

(Nanjing) A message from Tokyo on the 21st said that because Japanese bonds and the price of Japanese currency have fallen sharply in foreign markets since the Manchurian incident, Japanese Minister of Finance Inoue, with the consent of the Japanese cabinet on the afternoon of the 20th, issued a declaration saying that anyone familiar with the recent Manchurian incident knows that the Japanese army is acting entirely in self-defense. Japan obtained the police power in the South Manchuria Railway area from the Russo-Japanese Treaty of 1905, and this treaty was recognized by China. This situation is exactly the same as the United States having police power in the Panama Canal area, etc. Inoue issued this declaration in order to mislead the world and deliberately compared the situation with the United States in Panama. A reporter from the Central News Agency specially consulted a famous figure in diplomatic circles and asked for his views. According to him, Inoue's actions can be described as completely sophistry. Although the 1905 treaty recognizes the Japanese government's right to protect the South Manchuria Railway, it is by no means unrestricted deployment of troops. As for occupying Chinese cities and disarming the Chinese army because of the South Manchuria Railway, it is definitely not permitted by the treaty. Moreover, the scope of the Japanese army's occupation this time, including the northwest and Liaoyuan and Taonan, and the northeast and Jilin and Dunhua, is thousands of miles away from the South Manchuria Railway and has nothing to do with the 1905 treaty. Although the Japanese want to shirk responsibility through sophistry, the countries of the world will definitely not be deceived. To draw a comparison with the United States is even more inappropriate. Although the management right of the Panama Canal is in the hands of the United States, has the United States ever sent troops to occupy Panamanian territory? This further proves that the Japanese side is wrong. (Central News Agency Telegram, 22nd)

International News

French Prime Minister Arrives in Washington

The War Debt Problem is the Focus of Discussion

Reuters, New York, 22nd - French Prime Minister Laval arrived here today to a warm welcome. A 19-gun salute was fired. After landing, he was greeted by local officials and briefly rested for a few minutes. He then planned to take a train to Washington. It is reported that the discussions with President Hoover will focus on the gold issue, war debts, and armament burdens. He will depart for his home country on October 26. According to his statement to a special Associated Press correspondent on the Ile de France, France is not in a position to agree to a proposal to reduce war debts by half.

Britain Repays Loans to the United States

Japan Ships Large Amounts of Cash to the United States

Reuters, New York, 22nd - In August of this year, Britain borrowed heavily from France and the United States to replenish its reserves due to a large outflow of gold. A total of US$125 million was used by the Federal Reserve Bank of the United States. After Britain suspended the gold standard, the United States believed that this loan would become a bad debt within a certain period of time. However, Britain has now repaid US$100 million. The Federal Reserve Bank issued a report today expressing surprise at this action by Britain.

Reuters, Tokyo, 22nd - The Yokohama Specie Bank today shipped cash to the United States again. On October 29 and November 5, another 15 million yen worth of cash will be loaded onto ships and transported to the United States. Since October 3, Japan's cash outflow will total 135 million yen.

Japanese Extraordinary Cabinet Meeting

Discussing How to Deal With League of Nations Issues

Prince Saionji Will Go to Tokyo on the 26th

All cabinet members, from Prime Minister Wakatsuki down, attended. Opinions were exchanged on this matter, and the result was unanimous approval without any objection. Then, a report was given on the experiences of the League of Nations Council and on the sideline observations of the meeting.

More Than One Million Tons of Japanese Ships are Laid Up Amidst Anti-Japanese Sentiment

Small and Medium-Sized Industries are Shutting Down One After Another

Labor Disputes are Rapidly Increasing

Japan Associated Press, Tokyo, 22nd - Due to the depreciation of the British pound, the Japanese shipping industry is finding it impossible to make ends meet on long-distance voyages. Therefore, all ships are being used on coastal routes. However, there are too many ships in the inland sea, and exports have declined due to the Chinese insistence on anti-Japanese sentiment. More than one million tons of ships have been laid up, causing great panic among small-capital shipping companies.

The World Society reported, according to the Dongbao, that Osaka Prefecture, which is known as the number one in trade with China, has seen a shocking number of small and medium-sized industrialists shut down factories due to the stagnation of exports to China after the Eastern Provinces Incident and the intense anti-Japanese sentiment. Therefore, in the first 14 days of October alone, there were an average of two or three labor disputes per day. There are more than 40 disputes currently in progress, such as the Ito Enamel Company in Izumio Hirao Street, Osaka Lane. Police Officer Itano of the Special Higher Police Section of the Osaka Prefecture and other staff members are extremely busy. The factories that have fallen into this tragic situation specialize in glass, enamel, umbrellas, and other miscellaneous goods, with small and medium-sized industries employing 40 to 200 workers. At the same time, about 800 weaving factories of all sizes in the Izumi North and West Counties, the origin of Izumi textiles, are also in the same predicament. In particular, the cotton and woolen cloth and towel factories have seen a rapid succession of closures recently. For example, the cotton and woolen cloth weaving industry association in the jurisdiction of the Otsu Police Station decided on the 14th to suspend work for half a month each in October and November. The future direction is still uncertain. Furthermore, after discussions, the Izumi North Textile Industry Association of Sano mostly advocates suspending work or reducing production by 25%.

Japan Reforms Military System Budget

29 Million Yen

Japan Associated Press, Tokyo, 22nd - The Army has submitted a budget proposal to the Ministry of Finance for the implementation of military reforms. In order to carry out the reforms, they are requesting a seven-year plan for temporary expenses of 29 million yen. Among them, 18 million yen is required for the temporary expenses of transferring Japanese mainland divisions to Korea, abolishing the rotation system of divisions stationed in Manchuria and changing it to a permanent stationing system, and adding engineering corps to the Taiwan garrison.

Important News

Japanese Soldiers Confess the Truth About Bombing Jinzhou

The Bombing of Jinzhou Was Ordered by Honjo

The Targets for Bombing Were All Predetermined

Tianjin Communication - The incident of Japanese military aircraft bombing Jin County has attracted worldwide attention. According to a conversation with someone who returned to Tianjin from Shenyang yesterday, on the 9th of this month, the Manchuria Daily published an account by Major Yokota of the Japanese Army, who led the Japanese air squadron that bombed Jinzhou, revealing the beginning and end of the bombing, which is tantamount to a confession of a planned atrocity by the Japanese army. Unfortunately, the Manchuria Daily was confiscated by the Japanese military authorities and was not allowed to be published, so outsiders rarely see it. The main points of Yokota's statement in the newspaper are as follows: "Our bombing of Jinzhou this time was all in accordance with a prior explicit order. This order was issued before the Japanese government announced that Chinese people had attacked Japanese troops. We were originally stationed in Changchun and suddenly received an order to transfer to Shenyang. We didn't know what was going on, so the four aircraft in Changchun flew to Shenyang. After arriving in Shenyang, we received another order to combine with the eight aircraft in Shenyang, forming a temporary air squadron of twelve aircraft. Then, the squadron was divided into four teams of three aircraft each. Before the flight, the Kwantung Army Command gave us a map and designated four bombing destinations: Zhang Zuoxiang's residence, Jin County Jiaotong University, and two large camps of the Jin County garrison. After flying to Jinzhou, I dropped a total of eight bombs within fifteen minutes. The last bomb landed on the roof of Zhang Zuoxiang's residence," and so on. It was also stated that inspections are now extremely strict in Shenyang. Newspapers, photo studios, post offices, telegraph offices, and telephone offices are thoroughly inspected by the Japanese every day. Residents of Shenyang are also frequently inspected. This work is carried out by Japanese veterans in cooperation with regular soldiers. Many Japanese who have exceeded the age limit for veterans have also joined the effort. The Japanese army also led about thirty workers at 7:00 a.m. on the 11th of this month to completely dismantle the No. 1 and No. 3 intersections on the west end of the Dabeimen Railway Station in Shenyang, and removed about 200 feet of track. They then laid a new track from the intersection of the No. 3 intersection, connecting it to the joint transport line of the South Manchuria Railway. It has been completely completed. For several days, South Manchuria Railway locomotives have been pulling several empty cars, passing from the South Manchuria Railway through the Shenhai-South Manchuria joint transport line, passing the newly laid track, passing the East Station of Dabeimen and turning onto the branch line of the Beining Railway's arsenal, heading directly to the arsenal to load the military equipment stored in the factory.

Japanese Incitement of Illegal Organizations Intensifies

Establishing the So-Called Sino-Manchurian Province

Promoting a Small-Scale Autonomy Movement

Tianjin Correspondence: Since Japan occupied various areas of Liaoning and Jilin, it has been actively inciting their independence. Recently, realizing that a comprehensive movement is difficult to achieve, they have shifted to a so-called "small-scale autonomy" strategy, starting from individual counties. They have already carved out six counties—Lishu, Changtu, Kaiyuan, Huai'de, Tongliao, and Liaoyuan—from Liaoning Province to establish a separate Sino-Manchurian Province. The inherent territory of these six counties forms the province's domain, with Sipingjie as its capital. Kan Chaoxi's younger brother, Kan Chaoshan, has been appointed as the chairman of the Sino-Manchurian Province. He is currently visiting various counties to take over. Kan Chaoshan also serves concurrently as the chairman of Lishu County. Meng Zhongwen and Han Yinjie have been appointed as vice-chairmen. Li Ziyu, Zhu Shi'en, Liu Jingpu, a Mr. Dong, a Mr. Li, Yang Zhuchen, Wang Ji'an, Wang Gan'chen, Shi Youshan, Bi Huaxuan, Yue Junwu, Song Yindong, Li Yinsan, Fan Daquan, Zhang Shaowei, and twenty-one others serve as committee members, implementing the so-called autonomy system. Sipingjie has also been renamed as a city, with Kan Chaoshan concurrently serving as its mayor. Furthermore, Fushun and Tieling have also announced their autonomy one after another. Fushun began implementing autonomy on October 11th, with Xia Xuan as the chairman of the People's Autonomy Association, Liu Hanqing as the vice-chairman, and Jia Hanqing, He Xizhuo, and Sun Zhenkui as committee members. Tang Zhiming serves as the executive committee member. Japanese individuals, Yamaguchi Fumio and Komi Kaoru, have been hired as advisors. At noon on that day, the words "Fushun County People's Autonomy Association" were prominently written on the walls of the Fushun County Office. A yellow flag was raised, and a declaration and proclamation regarding the establishment of the autonomy association were distributed, stating that "The Fushun County People's Autonomy Association, in order to alleviate the suffering of the people and ensure their right to survival, hereby abolishes the local system of military dictatorship and county administration. A new people's autonomy, based on the traditional clan system of Chinese society, is hereby declared to administer local affairs." In Tieling, the existing Tieling County Government was abolished on the 9th of this month, and the sign of the Liaoning Province Autonomy Association was displayed. Simultaneously, influential officials and civilians within the city were convened to begin organizing an autonomous association, issuing a declaration stating, "This autonomy association, for the benefit of the people, abolishes the county government, the ruling apparatus of the old warlords, and restores the traditional Chinese autonomous system." Former county magistrate Yu Rongqing was appointed as the chairman, former public security chief Zhang Zuyin as the vice-chairman, former agricultural association chairman Yu Pan, vice-chairman Shi Jikui, former commerce association chairman Chang Yudong, former education bureau chief Zheng Lu, former diplomatic secretary Lin Shuzhi, Fu Wenhua, the head of Fuhe Hospital, and Zeng Qingchen, Wu Guihua, Shi Zhizhang, Wei Laige, Wang Zhegui, Yang Xuan, Hu Shixing, Deng Shiren, Fang Zuoqing, Wang Yuheng, Zhang Xulai, Yang Chunlin, Zheng Shizhang, Zeng Zhaoming, Huang Enhou, and Wu Changan serve as committee members. Yu Rongqing, Zhang Zuyin, Chang Bangdong, Yu Pan, Zheng Lu, Lin Shuzhi, Fu Wenhua, Shi Zhizhang, Yang Xuan, Hu Shixing, Deng Shiren, and Wu Changan serve as the executive committee members of Tieling. Japanese individuals, Kito Yoshiya (of the Commerce Association), Nishio Shin (chief of the People's Association), Misuhiro Eiji (vice-chairman of the South Manchurian Railway Local Committee), Yamada Keizo (vice-chairman of the Commerce Council), and Sato Fukujiro (specialty products merchant), have been hired as advisors. The so-called "small-scale autonomy" movement has already emerged in various counties of Liaoning, and Japan's incitement efforts have gradually succeeded. It is lamentable that there are so many Chinese Li Wanyongs. It is hardly surprising that a country with so many traitors will not perish.

Jinzhou Correspondence: After our exposure of the Japanese devil's conspiracy to incite the independence of Liaoning and Jilin provinces, they have recently intensified their efforts, using the same despicable methods, to actively proceed in various counties. The Liaoning Provincial Government recently reported based on reports from counties such as Tieling that the Japanese are even using false pretenses to draft so-called People's Autonomy Association regulations, forcibly requiring counties occupied by the Japanese devils to organize accordingly. The regulations consist of nine articles. Judging from the wording and content, they are clearly fabricated by the Japanese. The greatest objective within is to make each county independent, dividing the integrity of our sovereignty, and to exploit the weakness of our people's clan concepts, in order to achieve their conspiracy of manipulation and direction. They even recklessly use terms such as "revolution" and "warlords" to confuse our people's consciousness and falsely claim to abolish taxes, in order to ease our people's hostility towards them. Although their methods are extremely despicable, their intentions are indeed extremely sinister. Here are the so-called People's Autonomy Association regulations, copied verbatim, to see a glimpse of the Japanese conspiracy:

Pseudo-People's Autonomy Association Regulations (1) Spirit: Supreme and boundless. (2) Purpose: To create a rational organization and seek a fair and stable life for humanity. (3) Policy: To organize people's autonomy associations in various places, based on the people's perspective and regional units, and to exercise the people's right to survival. (4) Principles: 1. The people each retain the right to survival and the recognition of the right to mutual survival. 2. To retain freedom of religion and speech and to be responsible to all of humanity. 3. To retain the people's equal autonomy and all political powers. 4. The people must immediately sever relations with the evil government and evil forces. 5. The people must recognize the social tradition of Chinese clans. (5) Organization: 1. Organize with the people residing within the area where this association is established. 2. Nine people form a group, and the group is named after the group leader. 3. Nine small groups form a medium group, and the group is named after the medium group leader. 4. Nine medium groups form a large group, and the group is named after the large group leader. 5. Above the large group, the county serves as the autonomy association. (6) Autonomous Political Program: Abolish the evil military system since the Republic of China and restore the traditional clan system of China. (7) Organs: 1. The county autonomy association establishes an executive committee. The county executive committee establishes an autonomy bureau and a people's autonomous army. 1. The autonomous federation establishes a representative assembly. (8) Duties of Executive Committee Members: 1. To exercise all tasks related to the right to survival, based on the principles decided by the assembly. 2. To command the autonomous army. 3. To temporarily act on county affairs, including administration, finance, justice, and security. 4. To convene assembly affairs. (9) County Autonomy Bureau: 1. The county autonomy bureau is subordinate to the executive committee. 1. The county autonomy bureau carries out all temporary county affairs. 1. The executive committee determines the organizational and functional regulations of the county autonomy bureau. 1. The autonomy bureau houses an administrative department, a finance department, a judicial department, an education department, a police department, a general affairs department, and a supervisory department. "Note" 1. For the functions of the autonomy bureau and other temporary matters, useless insurance bureau matters are abolished and combined with the old functions. 2. Urgently establish the organizational regulations for the autonomous army. 3. Recruitment of autonomy association members, with executive cadres running around. 4. The police auxiliary body is to organize a defense team by conscripting local strong men, placed under the control of the autonomy bureau's police security. 5. For rural villages, issue set autonomy announcements. 6. The temporary executive committee is to make the following resolutions: 1. Abolish all taxes levied by warlords on the people since the past. 2. Newly establish an autonomous tax based on the old local surcharges, and self-defense fees. 3. The scope of tax abolition does not conflict with foreign treaties. 7. The conference proclaims that the establishment of the autonomy system is a people-saving revolution.

The 166th Central Executive Committee Meeting on the 22nd

Regulations on the Number of Executive and Supervisory Committee Members for the Hubei Provincial Party Department

Central News Agency Erroneously Releases News and is Punished

The 166th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee was held at 8:00 AM on the 22nd at the first conference hall of the Central Party Headquarters. Attendees included Ye Chucang, Ding Weifen, Chen Guofu, and Dai Chuanxian. Observers included Chen Lifu, Chen Zhaoying, Zhu Jiahua, Fang Juehui, Kong Xiangxi, Yang Shuzhuang, Wu Jingheng, Cheng Tianfang, Yu Jingtang, and Wang Boqun. Ding Weifen chaired the meeting. The resolutions are as follows: (1) Approval for the Hubei Provincial Party Department to convene a provincial representative assembly, and the number of executive committee members for the province is set at seven, with five alternate executive committee members, five supervisory committee members, and two alternate supervisory committee members. Double the required number should be elected in accordance with Article 2, Item C of the Provincial Executive and Supervisory Committee Member Election Outline, and submitted to the Central Committee for approval. (2) Approval for the Wuhan-Changsha-Zhuzhou-Pingxiang Railway Special Party Department to convene a full-line representative assembly on November 1st. The executive committee members for the party department are set at five, with three alternate executive committee members, three supervisory committee members, and one alternate supervisory committee member. Double the required number should be directly elected by the party on the line and submitted to the Central Committee for approval. (3) The resignation of Yunnan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee member Li Dianzhang is approved. The vacancy will be filled by Yang Wenqing. (4) Zhu Yaohua, Wang Jianbo, Yi Zhenxiang, Yu Jingyuan, Tang Pu, Xu Yeda, and Mo Yunxuan are designated as seven executive committee members for the Special Party Department of the 18th Division of the Army. Zhu Shifen, Gu Yizhang, and Lu Weiping are designated as three alternate executive committee members. (5) Lu Xiaochen, Wang Jinwen, Li Kun, Wang Weilin, Gao Jianlong, Liang Wenxian, and Long Ciyun are appointed as seven preparatory committee members for the Special Party Department of the 79th Division of the Army. (6) Regarding the Central News Agency's erroneous release of international news, which caused various misunderstandings in society, Deputy Director of the Central Propaganda Department Chen Bulei and Cheng Tianfang are to be warned. The person in charge of the Central News Agency is to be investigated by the Propaganda Department and severely punished. (7) Articles 12 and 18 of the Regulations on the Qualification Review and Examination of Central Party Headquarters Staff and Provincial or Special City Party Headquarters Overseas General Branch Committee Members and Staff are revised. (8) Central Committee members of the Overseas Students Management Committee Qiu Jingni and Fan Qi have not attended meetings for a long time. Wu Baofeng and Wang Qijiang are appointed as replacements. (9) Chen Songnian is appointed as the director of the Accounting Section of the Central Secretariat. (10) Hu Yiguan is appointed as the director of the Party Ideology Education Section of the Central Training Department. (11) Committee member Dai Chuanxian is recommended to present a report at the Central Commemoration Week next Monday.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

The Anti-Japanese Association Requests Identification of Foreign Yarn. Since the establishment of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in this county, investigators have been checking enemy goods at various ferry terminals. If suspected items are found, they are brought back to the Anti-Japanese Association for disposal. Yesterday (21st) afternoon, the Shanghai express train carried four large pieces of yarn, packed by the Shanghai Wansheng Mercerizing Factory, to the Yihe Socks Factory in Songjiang. The investigators noticed that the brand of the yarn was indeed produced by a Chinese factory, but the brand was pasted on separately, and there were traces of it being used before. The quality of the yarn was excellent, unlike domestic products, which was quite suspicious, so it was hired a cart to carry it back to the Anti-Japanese Association for disposal. Samples of the yarn were taken to various local sock factories, and everyone said that this kind of good goods did not seem to be domestic products, but it could not be definitively determined as enemy goods. Xu Xinmin was sent to Shanghai with the yarn samples to inquire at various factories and to ask the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to send personnel for precise identification. The yarn consisted of four large pieces, totaling one hundred and sixty packages. It is heard that another ten small packages of yarn belonging to the Zhenhe Factory, similar in quality to the Yihe Factory yarn, were seized in front of the court today.

Suzhou

The Min Surname Robbery Case Solved. Min Caichen, a trauma doctor in Sucheng Cang Street, also has a clinic outside the South Gate of Kunshan. On the afternoon of the previous day (21st), a bandit ship suddenly arrived, and six bandits entered and robbed the place. After seizing the loot, they took the ship and fled towards Suzhou. The 13th Kunshan Water Police team sent personnel to track and pursue them to Suzhou. The bandits in this case stayed at Room 26 of the Sanxin Inn on Liumen Road that night. Yesterday (22nd) morning, four bandits went to the station to take a train to Shanghai, when water police detectives Zhou Hongqing, together with the station military police, stepped forward and arrested them. According to their confessions, their names were Chen Wenhua, Lu Longxing, Ye Delu, and Jiang A'jin. They, along with the stolen goods, were taken back to Kunshan by the military police for interrogation.

Police and Bandits Exchange Fire, Rescuing a Large Number of Hostages. After the kidnapping case in Mochen Town, Changshu, Shen, the district chief of the 3rd Water Public Security District here, immediately ordered each team to step up arrests. The 14th team stationed in Wujiang and the 15th team stationed in Pingwang met more than one hundred bandits who looted Mochen, driving more than ten boats, at the junction of Tongli and Bei㘮 at about 7 pm on the 21st. The water police immediately opened fire, and the bandits also returned fire. The two sides held each other for three hours. The bandits retreated due to insufficient ammunition. At that time, three bandit ships were intercepted, and twelve male and female hostages were rescued. After receiving reports from each team yesterday (22nd), District Chief Shen personally took the Pei Rong battleship, leading a ship of teachers, and rushed to Zhouzhuang at 4 pm. At the same time, he ordered the 12th and 13th teams to set off immediately to encircle and suppress.

Changshu

Nearly 300 Pieces of Enemy Goods Seized from Three Silk Shops. Yesterday (20th) afternoon at 3 pm, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of this county, led by Anti-Japanese Association Chairman Shen Zuguang and Investigation Directors Li Junyuan and Yang Yongzhi, went to various silk bureaus to search. They first went to the Tongfuchang Silk Bureau on County South Street, where they seized 158 pieces of unregistered foreign goods. Then they went to Gantaiheng on County West Street and seized 52 pieces, and Yongfeng 80 pieces, totaling 289 pieces. Three yellow rickshaws were used to transport them to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Center of the County Party Headquarters for sealing. The Silk Fabric Industry Association specially convened an emergency meeting overnight. As a result, Miao Chongjie, Wu Hongfan, Ren Qingyuan, and Feng Yiwen were selected to go to the Anti-Japanese Association, meet with Committee Member Shen, and request the return of these unregistered enemy goods for registration, because the procedure had not been clearly understood beforehand, and even zero pieces were included in the registration example. Moreover, after discussing with Anti-Japanese Association Committee Member Lu Gongquan, he had agreed not to register anymore. Shen replied that the goods that had been investigated must be approved by a meeting before there would be a solution, and that the contact with Lu Gongquan was a private matter, and Lu could not control the power of the entire association. Later, the four representatives also asked whether they could stop the search starting from tomorrow (21st) and let each store take out Japanese goods themselves, listing them alongside domestic goods so that customers could pay attention. The four representatives then left.

Wuxi

A Large Batch of Japanese Goods Seized from Xiechengyong. The Inspection Department of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association received a tip that the residence at No. 20 Donghetou Lane in the city contained Japanese cloth goods from Xiechengyong, guarded by two apprentices from the store. The department immediately sent investigators to verify that it was true. Minister Wang Ciqing led inspectors to the scene and notified Xiechengyong and the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau to send police to assist in opening the lock. More than one hundred and several items of flower velvet, white velvet, flannel, and printed silk were found in the attic, waiting to be transported to the Anti-Japanese Association. Soon, many silk and cloth shop staff arrived, demanding that the goods be sealed up by the Chamber of Commerce. After a long argument, the party, government, and business sides agreed to temporarily seal the area by the Anti-Japanese Association. Unexpectedly, many workers suddenly demanded in the afternoon that the Anti-Japanese Association deposit the goods in the Anti-Japanese Association and strictly dispose of them. Li Tiping, Hu Nianqian, and Li Pu of the Anti-Japanese Association went to the Chamber of Commerce to discuss a solution. At that time, the masses had automatically rushed to Donghetou Lane to retrieve the goods, and the situation was extremely tense. In the evening, representatives from various related industries were elected to petition the county party headquarters and put forward three points: (1) All industries have already stopped buying and selling Japanese goods. The goods seized now were all purchased before the incident and have already been sealed. They should be re-registered. (2) Improve inspection methods. Before the deadline for re-registration, request a temporary suspension of inspections of residences and warehouses to maintain tranquility. (3) After the goods are sealed, they must be guaranteed, and the goods are all purchased by deposit or bank loans. It is winter and affects local finances. Request relief measures to maintain the commercial market. The county party committee members have agreed to consider and decide on a solution.

Nantong

The Issue of the Sulo Army's Land is Addressed. The Ministry of Military Administration ordered the county government to dispose of the military land of the old Sutown Langshan two battalions. County Magistrate Zhang informed the manager of the Tonghai Reclamation and Animal Husbandry Company, asking whether they were willing to pay the price or listen to the ministry's public sale. The company strongly opposed, stating that the military land had long been invested in the company and there was no illegal occupation. The county government has submitted it to the ministry for review.

Hangzhou

Miaoxi Temple is Robbed by Bandits. On the 20th, Miaoxi Temple in the southwest of Wuxing was suddenly invaded by two hundred bandits from Liangxing and Heping Town. They had machine guns and wooden-cased rifles, surrounded the defense team and seized more than one hundred firearms. The entire town was robbed, and squad leader Cheng Gongshou and team member Pan Zhengshou were killed. Several hundred people have gathered again in Bianshanwu. The Changxing County Magistrate telegraphed the province for emergency help. The provincial government flew a telegram to the stationed troops to suppress the bandits.

Gaoyitai Seizes Ten Thousand Pieces of Japanese Goods. Hangzhou Gaoyitai is the largest and most famous cloth shop in the city. On the 22nd, the Anti-Japanese Association of All Circles received a tip that it had a collection of Japanese goods worth 300,000 yuan. The association telegraphed and invited 400 armed volunteers from the Institute of Technology to surround the shop. More than ten thousand pieces of Japanese goods labels were found in the warehouse. After checking the cloth in the main store one by one, more than one thousand bolts of Japanese cloth were found. The Anti-Japanese Association has now convened an emergency meeting to severely warn the shop.

Jiaxing

Wangdian Gentry Fu Xu Jinlan is Kidnapped. After the routine temple fair in Wangdian Town, Jiaxing, a class was opened to perform operas to repay the gods. The town's public security bureau did not stop them. At about 8 pm on the 20th, while the performance was in full swing, six or seven bandits armed with pistols went to the Xishi Zushengchang Hotel and forcibly kidnapped the wealthy gentry Xu Jinlan, who was drinking in the shop. They got on a small boat that had been parked there in advance and sailed south. The 6th Water Police Team stationed in the town immediately gathered police officers and pursued them in different directions. At the same time, the land police and anti-smuggling battalion set out to encircle them. They encountered the bandit ship in Kaijing Port. The two sides opened fire. The bandits knew they were no match and abandoned the ship and hostages to escape ashore. Therefore, Xu Jinlan was taken back to the team headquarters by the water police and escorted home. The police are also following up on the case to strictly investigate the bandits.

Educational News Highlights

The Ministry of Education Promulgates the Principles for Implementing the Three People's Principles Education (5)

1. Based on the Party's teacher education aims and using training methods to guide their entire lives.

2. Through intellectual guidance and the earnest instructions of various commemorative gatherings, to cultivate their clear understanding and firm belief in the Three People's Principles.

3. To instruct the true meaning of education to save the country and the spirit of Chinese and foreign educators who dedicated themselves to education, to strengthen their lifelong commitment to the cause of education.

4. To awaken their love of the country and promote the spirit of the nation by promoting national morality and instilling national consciousness.

5. To train their healthy physique, regulated life, and the habit of perseverance and hard work through military training and sports competitions.

6. To cultivate their ability to thoroughly explore and observe precisely through scientific research experiments and the strict implementation of academic performance reviews.

7. To cultivate their frugal habits and group interest through various thrift movements and cooperative business guidance.

8. To cultivate their aesthetic emotions through proper entertainment and moderate outdoor travel.

9. To awaken their responsibility to improve family life through guidance on family ethical concepts and encouragement of labor operations (especially for female students).

10. To cultivate their ability to use the four powers and other preparations for civic life through student student self-government associations and other group business guidance.

(3) Equipment

1. All equipment should express the spirit of the Three People's Principles to the extent possible, and meet the conditions of simplicity and applicability.

2. All equipment should be related to training and teaching, and especially have considerable contact with the equipment of the experimental school and the experimental area.

3. All facilities should be adapted to the needs of society and should be opened as appropriate for public observation or use.

4. In addition to following the facilities of general schools, all equipment should pay attention to the arrangement of educational masters' portraits and should make Dr. Sun Yat-sen's legacy on education into school mottos and creeds.

5. Regarding books and equipment, attention should be paid to party ideology and education, and children's books should be prepared for students to study.

Chapter 5 Social Education

Section 1 Objectives

1. Improve public knowledge to equip them with common sense of modern urban and rural life.

2. Enhance public vocational skills to improve family economics and increase social productivity.

3. Train the public to be familiar with the four powers, implement self-government, and cultivate the national morals of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace, to cultivate citizens under the Three People's Principles.

4. Pay attention to national sports and public entertainment to develop their sound body and mind.

5. Cultivate social education cadres to develop the social education cause.

Section 2 Implementation Outline (1) Public School

A. Curriculum

1. The Three People's Principles should be the center of compiling the entire curriculum and teaching materials.

2. Adapt to local needs and production conditions to develop special courses and teaching materials.

3. Use more patriotic teaching materials to inspire the public's patriotic thoughts. 4. The curriculum of adult classes should pay attention to vocational common sense.

4. The curriculum of children's classes should pay attention to specific facts and use less abstract theories.

No Pension Regulations for Social Education Staff

Can be Handled in Accordance with the Regulations on Pensions for Officials

The Ministry of Education has been submitted by the director of the Fujian 甌 County Public Library requesting an explanation of whether social education staff enjoy the same treatment as school staff in pension and pension regulations. The Ministry of Education's instructions are as follows: The regulations on pensions for school staff are only applicable to school staff. The condolences for social education institutions staff are handled in accordance with the Ministry's established procedures and regulations on pensions for officials. Be aware of this.

Two Western Professors from Central University Arrive in Beijing

Nanjing Central News Agency Elects. In order to communicate world culture, the UNESCO Committee agreed with Central University this spring to exchange professors and has hired English literature professor Dr. Dewe from England and geological expert Dr. Bailey. On the 21st, they arrived in Beijing from Shanghai. Zhu Jiahua sent staff to receive them and find accommodation. The two are scheduled to discuss with the deans of the liberal arts colleges on the 22nd. Classes can be taught a week later. Due to various reasons, it is difficult to realize the dispatch of Chinese personnel at this time.

Local News

Ministry of Education Orders Students Returning from Japan in Shanghai to Wait Quietly for the Finalization of Transfer Procedures

The Ministry of Education specially appointed Councilor Zhu and Inspector Lin to Shanghai to handle the placement of students returning from Japan and ordered Director Xu of the Municipal Education Bureau to handle the registration matters together. It has already been announced that registration will begin in the Municipal Education Bureau on the 19th. It is now reported that Councilor Zhu and others have received a telegram from the Ministry, ordering them to instruct the students returning from Japan in Shanghai to wait quietly for the Ministry to determine the transfer procedures and must strictly abide by discipline and not be restless. The returning students have been notified to comply. (Education News Agency)

The City's Secondary School Anti-Japanese United Association

| Yesterday's Emergency Interim Executive Committee Meeting |

Three Measures Agreed Upon to Aid Students Forced to Leave the Sino-French School

Stopping Illegal Representative Congresses at Jinnan Affiliated Middle School and Other Schools

In Accordance With the Report of the City Party Headquarters Representative, Fundraising Departure Temporarily Postponed

Scheduled Expanded Propaganda, Six Schools Recommended to Meet With Guangdong Representatives

According to New Shanghai News, the Shanghai City Secondary School Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association held an emergency interim executive committee meeting at 2 PM yesterday at Minli Middle School near the Great South Gate regarding the Sino-French School expelling a large number of students. Attendees included representatives from Minli Middle School for Girls, Qingxin Middle School, Datong Affiliated Middle School, Jingye Middle School, Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, Daxia Affiliated Middle School, Xinmin Middle School, Meilun Middle School, Pudong Middle School, Shiyan Middle School, Fudan Affiliated Middle School, Dongwu No. 2 Middle School, Hujiang Affiliated Middle School, Minli Middle School, Chengzhong Middle School, Wuben Girls' Middle School, as well as over 30 representatives from the Sino-French School and a representative from the City Party Headquarters. Yu Zhongbiao and Datong Affiliated Middle School representative Hu Nianzhong were publicly elected as chairmen, and Minli Middle School for Girls representative Yi Bi as recorder. After the ceremony, (A) on reporting matters, the chairman reported that the emergency meeting was convened to discuss three important matters: (1) aiding students forced to leave the Sino-French School, (2) stopping illegal gatherings at Jinnan Affiliated Middle School, and (3) preserving the fundraising departure issue. Next, Sino-French School representative Ye Shuliang reported on the circumstances of being forced to leave the school, stating that the school had over 1,000 students and that its administration was purely based on religion, and that all academic subjects extremely emphasized French, akin to colonial education. This time, students were prohibited from holding patriotic movements and organizing anti-Japanese associations, and it was declared, "If you want to study at this school, you cannot be patriotic; if you want to be patriotic, you are not allowed to study at this school." Such absurd remarks were openly uttered by a French person. What is there to tolerate if this is tolerable? The students, with their ardent patriotism, intended to ignore it, but unexpectedly on the morning of the 20th, they were ordered to have all members of the over-grade and head-grade groups A and B leave the school, announced their expulsion, and were forced to leave the school. However, on one hand, they continued their efforts with a spirit of never giving up, and on the other hand, they hoped that the association would do its best to provide assistance so that the students would not have no place to study. (B) On discussion matters, (1) Regarding the case of students at the Sino-French School being expelled by the school authorities for organizing anti-Japanese associations, how should the association provide assistance? It was resolved (1) that the association should immediately request the City Education Bureau to negotiate with the French Consul in Shanghai; (2) that the association would recommend one standing member, plus three representatives from Fuzhong, Shizhong, and Wuben, to go to the Sino-French National Institute of Technology to request Principal Chu Minyi to allow them to transfer to that school; (3) that a declaration would be issued announcing the corrupt content of the school and advising future youths not to enter the school again. (2) Regarding the report from Datong Affiliated Middle School and other schools about Jinnan Affiliated Middle School and other schools holding illegal gatherings and scheduling representative congresses, how should the association stop them? It was resolved (1) to notify all schools not to participate; (2) to send letters to the four schools that had joined the association, namely, Shanghai North Middle School, Zhengfeng Middle School, Anhui Middle School, and Guohua Middle School, to question them; (3) to report to the City Party Headquarters to request a halt. (3) The association had previously scheduled to depart for fundraising on the 26th, but according to the report of the representative from the City Party Headquarters, the City Anti-Japanese Association already had concrete measures. Should the association still proceed as scheduled? It was resolved to preserve the issue and temporarily postpone it. (4) Regarding scheduling a citywide secondary school expanded propaganda campaign, it was resolved to set the date for Wednesday to Friday afternoon, with the address being one day in Shanghai and two days outside Shanghai, held simultaneously, with all expenses paid by the schools themselves. (5) Regarding the case of the association recommending representatives to pay respects to Mr. Wang Jingwei, it was resolved to recommend representatives from Minli Middle School for Girls, Wuben Girls' Middle School, Fudan Affiliated Middle School, Datong Affiliated Middle School, Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, and Jingye Middle School to go on the morning of the 23rd (today). (6) Regarding the case of regulating each school's duty to serve as a standing member of the association, it was resolved to stipulate that each school should pay five silver dollars per month, pending recognition and collection by the representative congress. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Departmental Meeting of the Military Training Department of the Anti-Japanese Association of Various Universities

Regulations for Divisional Inspections, Locations, and Times for Each School

The Military Training Department of the Shanghai Universities Student Anti-Japanese United Association held its third departmental meeting at the Youth Propaganda Corps at 3 PM yesterday. Attendees included Gu Jiwu from Jiangnan University, Liang Meichu from the Sino-French University, Chen Shichang from Hujiang University, and Wen Guangyi from Jinan University. The meeting was chaired by Wen Guangyi, Director of the Military Training Department, with Wu Baojin as recorder. After the ceremony, the discussion began. (1) It was resolved to regulate the divisional inspection locations and times for each school. The first district, first group, includes five schools: Labor University, Chizhi University, Culture University, Law School, Business University. The location is Fudan University, and the time is 9 AM on November 1. The second group includes four schools: Fudan University, Hujiang University, Art College, and Dongwu Law School. The location is Fudan University, and the time is 9 AM. The second district includes four schools: Sino-French University, Tongji University, Merchant Marine University, and Central Medical University. The location is the Sino-French University, and the time is 9 AM on the 5th. The third district includes six schools: Jinan University, Southeast Medical College, Daxia University, Guanghua University, St. John's University, Jiangnan University, and Zhengfeng University. The location is Daxia University, and the time is 9 AM on the 7th. The fourth district, first group, includes six schools: East Asia University, Daxia University, Political Science and Law University, Sino-French Institute of Technology, Sino-French Pharmaceutical College, and National Conservatory of Music. The location is the Public Stadium, and the time is 9 AM on the 9th. The second group includes eight schools: Jiaotong University, Aurora University, Tongde University, American Art College, National Medical College, Journalism College, Chinese Medical College, and Xinhua Lingyi College. The location is the Public Stadium, and the time is 9 AM on the 11th. (2) It was recommended to establish preparatory committees for divisional inspections and convene meetings. It was resolved that each school should send one person to organize the meetings. The designated conveners are Fudan University for the first district, Sino-French University for the second district, Daxia University for the third district, and Sino-French Institute of Technology for the fourth district. (3) It was regulated who the divisional commanders would be. It was resolved that the commanders would be Chizhi for the first district, first group; Hujiang for the second group; Sino-French for the second district; Jinan for the third district; Sino-French for the fourth district, first group; and Aurora for the second group. (4) Each school's volunteer army and ambulance team report forms are due to the Military Training Department by the 25th. (5) Four types of systems were compiled: general team, middle team, district team, and squad. (6) After the symbols are submitted by each school, they will be compiled and issued. (7) The headquarters will make the banners on behalf of each school, and each school should prepare funds to collect them. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Election of City Education Association Representatives by Two District Education Associations

Four People Elected in the Second District...Tenth District Schedules a Meeting

Second District The Second District Education Association of this city held its second membership meeting at the Municipal Tangmiao Elementary School at 3 PM the day before yesterday (the 21st) to elect representatives to attend the City Education Association's citywide representative congress. Over 50 members attended, as well as Mao Xiaxuan, a representative from the City Party Headquarters, and Chen Songchun, a representative from the City Education Bureau. Liu Yun was publicly elected as chairman, Wang Deyan as recorder, and Wang Lide as master of ceremonies. After the ceremony, the chairman first reported on the purpose of the meeting, and then representatives from the City Party Headquarters and the City Education Bureau successively delivered speeches. Then the election began, and as a result, Wang Dingcheng, Lu Yunqian, Mao Yun, and Liu Yun were elected as representatives to attend the city conference. The meeting adjourned immediately after.

Tenth District The Tenth District Education Association of this city, according to the resolution of the fourth executive committee meeting, has scheduled its second membership meeting for 2 PM on the 27th of this month at Shicun Elementary School in Pusong Town to elect representatives to the City Education Association. It is reported that all members have been notified to attend on time, and a request has been submitted to the City Party Headquarters, the preparatory committee of the City Education Association, and the City Education Bureau to send personnel to guide the meeting. Fifth Batch of Party Teacher Qualifications Approved in This City

The Third Batch of Lists to Be Announced Soon

The Shanghai Committee for Reviewing the Qualifications of Party Doctrine Teachers held its seventh regular meeting yesterday and approved the qualifications of approximately 167 high school, junior high school, and elementary school teachers recommended by various committees. There were also several cases of retention pending investigation or resolutions of disqualification. According to the yesterday's approved qualifications constitute the fifth batch, and the committee needs to hold one more meeting to completely conclude the remaining unfinished cases. The third batch of qualified lists is scheduled to be announced next Monday, and the certificates will also be issued within one month starting next Monday. The fourth batch of certificates is also being actively prepared.

Representatives of Various University Anti-Japanese National Salvation Associations Meet With Wang and Sun

According to Nichinichi Shimbun, yesterday morning at 9 AM, representatives from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Associations of various universities in this city, including Ji Shiyuan, Lu Zhaozhen, Xie Yanqing, Wen Guangyi, Wu Baojin, Zhu Youhuan, Cao Peizi, Nie Haifan, and others, went to pay respects to the Guangdong representatives. They were received by representatives Wang Jingwei and Sun Ke. The record of their conversation is as follows: (1) Asked about the student associations' advocacy of declaring war on Japan, what were the gentlemen's opinions? Wang replied that it had been discussed in Guangdong, and there was not only the final determination but also the necessary final preparations. (2) Asked about the issue of restoring diplomatic relations with Russia, what was the Guangdong side's position? Wang replied that it had not been discussed in Guangdong. (3) Asked about what the gentleman's personal attitude on the issue was. Wang replied that the Communist Party should be excluded, but diplomatic relations with Russia could be restored. However, in the past, the Russian consulate functioned as a communist organ, so it was necessary to search it. (4) Asked about the gentlemen's opinions on the issue of restoring civil rights. Sun replied that in principle, he absolutely agreed that revolution required the masses. Past failures were due to the lack of organization among the masses, which led to military command and politics resulting in a military dictatorship. The methods should be improved now. (5) Asked about the gentlemen's opinions on withdrawing from the League of Nations. Wang replied that he had said in a speech to the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in Guangdong on October 19 that he had no hope for the League of Nations. However, whether immediately withdrawing from the League of Nations would further isolate China internationally was a concern that needed to be considered. This was a diplomatic issue that should be discussed before a decision was made. (6) Asked about the gentleman's opinions on party affairs. Wang replied that the party should restore democratic centralism, and then politics could be democratically centralized. (7) Asked when he would have time to allow him to give a public speech. He replied that he was very busy now. Mr. Chiang Kai-shek would arrive today, and the date of the speech would be determined later. (8) Asked about the gentleman's opinions on the student movement. He replied that this was a long question to discuss. The most important thing was to build up strength. In the past, during the May Thirtieth and May Third incidents, it was not sustainable. Now, the focus should be on sustainability. After the major issues are resolved, it is hoped that the government can help the students. (9) Asked about the gentleman's opinions on the peace and unification conference. He replied that he had great hope for this conference. We came with great sincerity. There was no use. We hoped that the people would understand and that the comrades in Nanjing would understand, so that greater consultation could be successful, and so on.

Jinda Library Plans to Expand

Jinan University has added over 50,000 yuan in books in the past four years. The Hong Nian Library currently houses the following books: (1) General category: 8,685 volumes; (2) Philosophy category: 1,779 volumes; (3) Education category: 2,664 volumes; (4) Social Sciences category: 2,583 volumes; (5) Arts category: 1,497 volumes; (6) Natural Sciences category: 2,674 volumes; (7) Applied Sciences category: 1,632 volumes; (8) Language category: 2,437 volumes; (9) Literature category: 6,481 volumes, for a total of 33,766 volumes, of which 25,353 volumes are in Chinese and 8,513 volumes are in Western languages. The library's book design committee recently resolved to expand by adding at least 100,000 yuan in books within five years, to be carried out in stages. 10,000 yuan in books have already been advanced this year and are being shipped in succession. In addition, Principal Zheng Hongnian is currently residing in Zhenru, handling and improving various school affairs with exceptional busyness.

Shanghai Middle School's Fourth Anniversary Yesterday

Provincial Shanghai Middle School in Nanshi, this city, held its fourth anniversary celebration yesterday. The commemorative meeting was held at 9 AM in the gymnasium of the junior high school department. Over 1,800 people attended, including teachers and staff of the school, students from the senior high school, junior high school, and experimental elementary school departments, as well as guests Hu Shuhua, President of Tongji University, Li Zhaohuan, President of Jiaotong University, and Xu Peihuang, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau. All students wore uniform uniforms. The meeting opened with music. After the ceremony, Principal Zheng Xige gave a speech, generally reporting on the past four years and stating that he would make special efforts in the future to consolidate the foundation of the school, research work, and youth training. Next, guests Hu Shuhua, Xu Peihuang, and Li Zhaohuan gave speeches in succession, mostly encouraging young people to study hard and save the country. Then, Wang Yungong, the school's music education teacher, performed a violin solo, and Tian Ding'an, a representative of the faculty and staff, and Chen Zhengzhang, a student representative, gave speeches in succession. Finally, there was photography, music, and the anti-Japanese association. At 2 PM, a review of the student army and boy scouts was held in the high school department's playground. The senior high school and junior high school students were in full military attire, full of energy. In addition to the school's faculty and staff, there were also many guests serving as reviewing officers. After the review, the boy scouts and students successively performed drills with lively movements and skillful execution, which was greatly praised by the guests. It was also heard that the school originally planned to hold an achievement exhibition and a carnival, but due to the sudden dispatch of troops by the brutal Japanese to invade and occupy our country's Northeast, all the teachers and students of the school are dedicated to anti-Japanese national salvation affairs, so they have temporarily postponed it.

The Tianma vs. Zejia Xiangbin Cup Final Tonight

Location: The Racing Club Tongren Clubhouse

The Xiangbin Cup competition, which stands out and is famous throughout the country, has a long history that has long been known in the sports world. The Tianma team has won the most championships in the past, dominating the scene for a time, having won three times in succession. The Jiande team, which is well-known in Shanghai, has only won the championship once in the second edition. Although the team had joined this year, it suddenly withdrew; otherwise, it would not have been difficult to compete with Tianma and Zejia for the Xiangbin Cup. According to the cup competition's regulations, whoever wins the championship four times in succession can permanently keep the cup. Therefore, the Tianma team will definitely show their skills this time to fight for honor and fulfill their long-cherished wish. However, the Zejia team has talented generals like clouds, which can be called a strong enemy. It is entirely possible to defeat Tianma. Therefore, the final between the two teams tonight will definitely be a fierce battle. Unfortunately, due to the brutal Japanese invasion and the country being in danger, the cup competition's organizing committee decided to adopt a tight policy, holding it at the clubhouse and not inviting any guests due to venue constraints, preventing those interested in this sport from watching. Special Article

Liu Haisu's Report to the Ministry of Education After Returning to China (5)

(1) The Organization and Establishment of Museums

Every major city and remote town in Europe has established museums to collect ancient and modern art relics and reproductions of masterpieces. This not only improves the aesthetic sense of the general public, but also provides resources for scholars and antiquarians to study. The collection and management have become specialized sciences. Therefore, all displays, cataloging, patching, and storage are carried out according to precise methods. As a result, they are well-ordered and magnificent. Ancient relic preservation sites exist in various parts of our country, but they are all perfunctory, with no reports or statistics, which clearly shows that they do not follow scientific methods. Moreover, there have been rumors from time to time that antiques have been stolen from various ancient relic exhibition sites, which is especially ridiculed by both Chinese and foreigners. Therefore, reorganizing existing museums and ancient relic preservation sites using scientific methods is a current urgent task. Furthermore, choose large cities with convenient transportation and high population density, such as Nanjing and Shanghai, to build large-scale museums, or expand existing preservation sites, or start and operate them in order to suit modern scales. All storage should prioritize treasures and genuine works. However, for famous works that cannot be moved but can be reproduced, such as statues from past dynasties and tomb gate reliefs related to art history, experts should be hired to reproduce them and distribute them to museums across the country, so that scholars everywhere can have convenient access to research and will not have to travel north and south to seek one object.

(2) The Establishment of the Republic of China Academy of Fine Arts

All European countries have established national academies of fine arts. In addition to France, the German state of Prussia is named the Akademie der Künste. The United Kingdom has the Royal Academy of Arts, and Belgium has the Royal Academy of Fine Arts. Japan also has the Imperial Academy of Art. Well-known scholars and famous artists are selected as members to plan the direction of art education and art social facilities, provide the state with advice on art, study proposals for art schools, music schools, and museums, and preside over national periodic art exhibitions to attract art awards and promote the rise and fall of art matters. Although the systems vary from country to country, the intention is the same. Given the profound historical foundation of our country and the large number of undertakings to be carried out, the establishment of a national academy of fine arts should not be allowed to be lacking. In today's era, all artistic undertakings cannot be transferred according to the trends of one person or one family, but must seek to align with the intentions of the entire society. All innovations must have a comprehensive plan in order to achieve twice the result with half the effort. People today often say that the economy is insufficient, but in fact, if there is a central organization to gather talent and plan and preside over it, being pragmatic and starting from the near and extending to the far, even a small amount of economy can become a large amount of undertaking. If one chokes and refuses to eat, then the backwardness of Chinese culture will never be able to revitalize itself. In Haisu's foolish opinion, the national academy of fine arts, the main focus of art facilities, is also a major institution that our country urgently wants to organize.

(3) The Improvement of the Art School System

Our country's art schools have recently set a three-year study period, which is comparable to the vocational schools of industry and commerce. However, a review of art schools in Europe shows that their goal is to cultivate advanced art experts, with no fixed time limit. Their research process is similar to that of universities. From Haisu's experience, it is felt that art schools are fundamentally different in nature from other vocational schools. Therefore, the three-year time limit is actually too short. Is it not ridiculous to apply the time limit for learning ordinary arithmetic, bookkeeping, and bookkeeping to those who study literature and philosophy? Although our country is currently in a transitional era, there is no need to seek perfection in everything. However, the distinction between high-level academic art and ordinary technology must be clarified. In the field of art schools, whether cultivating teachers or cultivating experts, they cannot be mentioned in the same breath as ordinary vocational technology. Even for the sake of meeting the urgent needs of society, for example, regarding teachers of music, painting, and handicrafts, who are expected to be quickly trained, they may be regarded as being the same as vocational technology. However, high-level academic art must be treated as a separate matter and cannot be mixed up. In Haisu's foolish opinion, the study period for art schools should be at least five years. The departments and systems for cultivating teachers may be slightly shortened. This is already a compromise compared to European countries. If you think that high-level academic art cannot be borrowed and that scholars should be spared from superficiality, then the improvement of the school system is a matter that cannot be delayed.

(4) The Necessity of Articulating Material Construction

In recent years, construction projects have been changing with each passing day in various parts of our country, and the increasing modernization of cities is a particularly prominent fact. During Haisu's travels in Europe, visiting cities of all sizes, I could not help but think about how each place has its own strengths. The display of these strengths to the people's eyes depends on the articulation of art in construction. The articulation of art in construction is not a difficult task. The key is for the designers to pay attention to the trends of the times and the circumstances of the location, arrange public and private buildings, and make organic coordination, avoiding all unreasonable and irregular forms, and everywhere taking being pleasing to the eye as the criterion, not seeking beauty but being beautiful. In the past, urban construction in our country was either presided over by foreigners or copied old chapters, so there was a strange hybrid style. Now, at a time when construction is progressing, we should pay attention to the principles of articulation of art, so that residents feel happy and views are appropriate, creating a model district in the East, which is what the authorities engaged in construction would be happy to hear.

Haisu's luggage has been unloaded in the south, and the first thoughts are varied. The above is a general outline, a preliminary presentation of what I can remember at the moment, to serve as a starting point. As for detailed reports and research insights, please allow me some time to continue organizing them so that the government and the people can take note of them together.

Chiang Kai-shek Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning

Sincere Unity to Face External Enemies

Chiang Returns to Nanjing by Plane in the Evening

Since the Guangdong representatives Wang Jingwei and others arrived in Shanghai and met with various committees in Nanjing, the methods for peaceful unification have been of general concern. It is learned that Chairman Chiang also arrived in Shanghai by plane yesterday morning and gathered at Sun Ke's residence at 2 PM in the afternoon for consultations. After the meeting, Chiang returned to Nanjing by plane. The results of the consultations and various circumstances are compiled and recorded separately as follows.

Consultations at Sun's Residence

Chairman Chiang arrived in Shanghai by plane from Nanjing at 10 AM yesterday morning and held the first meeting at Sun's residence at 10 Moliere Road at 2 PM yesterday afternoon. Key party and government figures such as Chiang Kai-shek, Hu Hanmin, Wang Jingwei, and Sun Ke gathered together to discuss matters harmoniously for about two hours. This meeting was of great importance to the safety and security of the party and the country. The initial results yesterday were satisfactory, and the future looked optimistic.

Attending Representatives

From Nanjing, Chiang Kai-shek, Yu Youren, Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Ji, Li Shizeng, Zhang Jingjiang, Chen Mingshu, and Shao Yuanchong. From Guangdong, Wang Jingwei, Sun Ke, Wu Chaoshu, Li Wenfan, Chen Youren, Zou Lu, and Hu Hanmin, totaling fifteen people.

Gathering at Song's Residence

Before the Nanjing and Guangdong representatives met yesterday, the Nanjing representatives first convened a talk at Song's residence on Seymour Road at around 12 PM. The attendees included Chiang Kai-shek, Zhang Ji, Cai Yuanpei, Li Shizeng, Wu Tiecheng, Yu Youren, Shao Yuanchong, Shao Lizi, Zhang Jingjiang, and Zhu Peide, totaling more than ten people. Zhang Ji and Cai Yuanpei Chen Mingshu served as intermediaries, traveling between Sun's residence on Moliere Road and Song's residence on Seymour Road to convey the necessary contacts between the two sides before they met. Zhang and Cai went to Sun's residence once at 12:30 PM for contact, and Chen Mingshu went to Sun's residence twice at 1:10 PM and 1:45 PM before deciding to officially meet at Sun's residence at 10 Moliere Road at 2 PM.

Meeting Scheduled

The six Guangdong representatives had lunch at Sun's residence yesterday afternoon. Upon learning that Chiang had arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing, Chiang sent someone to Sun's residence to notify them, and they agreed to meet at Sun's residence at 2 PM in the afternoon. At exactly 2 PM, Hu Hanmin arrived at Sun's residence first, and Chiang arrived at 2:15 PM. As for Yu Youren, Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Ji, Li Shizeng, Zhang Jingjiang, Chen Mingshu, and Shao Yuanchong, they were already seated. After meeting and exchanging greetings, they discussed peaceful unification and sincere unity, and other methods. At 4:30 PM, Chiang left first, and Zhang Jingjiang also left ten minutes later. Before long, Zhang Ji left with Yu Youren. Finally, Cai Yuanpei and Chen Mingshu also left Sun's residence one after another, while the six Guangdong representatives remained resting at Sun's residence.

Shaking Hands and Making Peace

After arriving at Sun's residence, Chiang first expressed his longing for the people who had come to Shanghai from Guangdong. Wang and others also exchanged pleasantries, shaking hands, and laughing, and they were very happy. Then, they discussed the importance of diplomatic issues and unity to jointly face the national crisis. Chiang earnestly expressed during the meeting that he hoped that his comrades would immediately go to Nanjing to jointly assume the important task of saving the country. All matters could be discussed in detail, and he would be happy to comply with anything that benefited the party and the country. Hu, Wang, Sun, Wu, and others spoke one after another, all believing that the realization of unity was extremely urgent. After chatting for one hour and twenty-five minutes, Chiang took his leave. According to a certain central committee member who participated in the talks, the impression of all parties at yesterday's talks was excellent. Sincere unity would definitely be achieved, but before entering Nanjing, there would be several more talks in Shanghai. It is heard that Zhang Jingjiang and Li Shizeng will participate.

Consultation Results

The consultation process was very good. After the consultation, the Guangdong side issued the following statement: The six Guangdong representatives still spoke based on their previous demands and explained that the purpose of their visit to Shanghai for consultations on peaceful unification was that the party, government, and military must undergo fundamental improvements and reforms. In other words, democratic politics must be established. Chiang expressed acceptance. After this sincere meeting between the two sides, two methods were decided: (1) In terms of diplomacy, a consensus must first be reached in order to jointly face the national crisis. (2) For issues such as party affairs, politics, and military affairs, Nanjing will appoint representatives to come to Shanghai to hold a preparatory meeting with the Guangdong representatives, jointly discuss detailed methods, and formulate a detailed draft. The draft will then be taken to Nanjing by the representatives of both sides to hold a formal meeting and make a final decision. The two sides, in view of previous mistakes, are determined to be especially cautious in future discussions.

Recommending Representatives

The representatives from Nanjing were originally Zhang Ji, Cai Yuanpei, and Chen Mingshu. However, the formal appointment must await approval by the Central Standing Committee.

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the National Government, accompanied by Central Committee member Chen Bu-lei, arrived in Shanghai at 10:20 AM yesterday, aboard a newly purchased American aircraft from Nanjing.
