Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement

The Municipal Party Department Submits a Telegram to the Central Government

Please Don't Let the Ambassador Yield in the League of Nations

The Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department telegraphed the Central Executive Committee in Nanjing yesterday: Since the violent Japanese destroyed international conventions, disregarded world peace, and sent troops to forcibly occupy the Eastern Provinces for a month, our people have been determined to save the country. In the midst of solemn endurance, they trust the government and wait quietly for the League of Nations to take concrete and effective measures in accordance with the conventions to uphold justice, stop violence, maintain its own life, and protect the peace of mankind. However, the League of Nations' hope that Japan will withdraw its troops has not been realized again and again, and Japan's fire in our territory is getting more and more fierce, and the destruction is getting worse. They have turned a blind eye to it. Recent news has come that Japan has proposed five principles for withdrawing troops, suggested it to Briand, and requested negotiations with our Ambassador Shi. At the same time, the League of Nations Council will postpone it for three weeks, authorizing Briand to mediate in order to complete the withdrawal of troops. The League of Nations is so protecting the powerful and deceiving and perfunctory, which is no less than yielding to Japan. The death penalty is self-announced. Our country should take self-defense actions and rise up to take responsibility for maintaining international conventions. Furthermore, the five principles for withdrawing troops proposed by Japan are extremely absurd. If this can be negotiated, it is tantamount to acknowledging the country-destroying treaty of 21 Articles. Our people are even more deeply angry. At this time of life and death, we must not be negligent and make mistakes. In the view of the Council, there are two points that must be insisted: (1) Japan's dispatch of troops to the Eastern Provinces is obviously an act of war. Unless Japan first withdraws troops unconditionally and acknowledges compensation for all damages, our country should never negotiate with it in any way, and it is not allowed to propose any counter-proposals for the so-called conditions for withdrawing troops. (2) If the League of Nations forces China to recognize any preconditions for Japan's withdrawal of troops, and any resolutions that violate the League of Nations Charter, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, or the Nine-Power Treaty, China should resolutely reject them, and please ask Ambassador Shi not to declare again, "China absolutely unconditionally obeys the League of Nations' decisions and actions," etc., so as not to put himself in a difficult situation. Time is urgent, so I especially telegraphed to you for verification and attention, and begged you to quickly give an order to Ambassador Shi to pay close attention to it in order to save the crisis. Otherwise, the diplomatic humiliation will ruin the country, and the sin will be traced to you. The Chinese Kuomintang Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee, with the utmost urgency, bows.

The Anti-Japanese Association Holds a Standing Committee Meeting

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of this city held its eleventh standing committee meeting yesterday. The committee members present were Lu Jingshi, Fang Jiaobo, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Yansong, Chairman Lin Kanghou, and Recorder Zhao Shusheng. The following cases were discussed: (1) The Cotton Cloth Trade Association notified its members to prevent inspection, and how should this be handled? It was resolved to transfer it to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to send a letter to the association to withdraw this notice. (2) The Inspection Department reported that Bao Daxiang privately hid enemy goods and colluded with French foreign firms to cover up. It was resolved to entrust the Investigation and Inspection Departments to jointly investigate and detain the goods with the Cotton Cloth Trade Association. (3) The accounts of the former Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee were requested to be verified and announced. It was resolved to appoint committee members Xi Yushu and Li Wenjie to review and report for verification. (4) The Investigation Department reported that the registration of Yitai Feng Company was inconsistent, and now a copy of the source of goods book is presented to the meeting. Zhang Yaozeng's Letter to the People of the Country

In the cooperative efforts of all nations in the world to create peace and reduce armaments, under the faith guarantee of the International League of Nations, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Nine-Power Treaty, Japan, which claims to be civilized, suddenly launched a large army, launched a surprise attack in the dark night, seized my famous cities, slaughtered my people, plundered my armaments, seized my political power, destroyed my transportation, and blockaded my finances. In two days, it plundered the capital and important places of my Chinese territory in the two provinces of Liaoning and Jilin for thousands of miles and placed them under artillery fire, letting them wreak havoc. This is truly unprecedented violence in history and a bomb to destroy human civilization. It is a fatal insult to my Chinese nation. My nation is in this tragic change, for the sake of its own survival, for the sake of human culture, rising up generously, exhausting all the spiritual power of my entire nation, rushing forward together, and doing everything possible to subdue the violent sun and support justice. This is not only the obligation of my nation to our ancestors, but also the inevitable mission to human culture. I believe that all my compatriots have deeply felt this obligation and this mission, and I also believe that all my compatriots will be able to sincerely practice it. However, Yaozeng is anxious and there is something I must respectfully tell all my compatriots: In the face of extraordinary changes, we must rely on extraordinary strength. Extraordinary strength cannot be produced without extraordinary unity. Extraordinary unity cannot be achieved without extraordinary awareness. My nation has been invaded by the violent sun for a long time, and the disasters have come one after another. It is not that we have not tried to resist it, but the resisters resist, and the invaders invade more and more. Now they are peeling off our skin and touching our bones, and in an instant, they reach our heart. This is because the resisters have no real strength, and the source of the chaos and weakness of my nation has not been eliminated. Please observe the Jiaoji Incident of the Japanese Kou in the 17th year of the Republic of China. It can be said to be a strange shame and humiliation. My people have sworn to resist it to the death, but what have we done in the past three or four years? Have we worked together to build a national defense against Japan? Have we cooperated sincerely to strengthen our domestic strength? No, we haven't. Because we have not, we have today's strange change. Today's crisis and danger are hundreds of times greater than before. The Chinese people's resistance and struggle are also hundreds of times greater than before. However, gnashing their teeth and roaring in anger, they cannot be said to have real strength. Real strength cannot be produced without consistent unity, vigorous progress, and unremitting efforts. We talk about unity, but everyone has their own biases and acts in their own self-interest. It cannot be said to be real unity. Real unity cannot be produced unless everyone is fully aware of their own mistakes in the past, deeply repents, and cherishes each other. Who is to blame for today's tragedy and humiliation of my nation? My nation is to blame. The celebrities of my nation have attacked, killed, and weakened the whole nation by their thoughts and actions, causing the whole nation to be chaotic and weak. Alas, even today, do we want to follow their thoughts and inherit their actions while talking about unity and saving the country in vain? I am afraid that my ancestor, the Yellow Emperor Xuanyuan, will not forgive me. Now, please each of my compatriots respectfully stand and silently pray, think deeply, and reflect deeply: Where is the source of the chaos and weakness of my nation? The source of chaos and weakness is in me: daring to be self-confident and positioning myself high, thinking that no one is like me in loving the country and saving the nation, and everyone should be used by me and should not resist me. Those who obey me must be protected, and those who are different from me must be removed, regardless of good or evil, and by any means. This is the source of chaos and weakness. Do I have this? Regarding the local area as an area for support, and holding the troops as a means of self-defense, I focus on enriching my military strength every day and expanding my territory as my goal. When I have the opportunity, I merge and attack, and when I lose power, I divide and occupy. I specialize in using various beautiful names to indulge my great desires and vent my personal anger. I do not care about the lives and property of my compatriots. I do not ask about faith, justice, law, and discipline. This is the source of chaos and weakness. Do I have this? Relying on the power of the country to run my own livelihood, accepting bribes and selling officials, embezzling public funds, and my personal life is extravagant, and I have many ways to increase my wealth. This is the source of chaos and weakness. (To be continued)

Stamp Banknotes with Anti-Japanese Symbols

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday notified the trade associations of various industries in this city, stating that there are many methods of economic severance with Japan. Adding a rubber stamp of "Do Not Buy Japanese Goods" to silver coins or paper money is even more striking. When using this silver coin or paper money, seeing the four characters "Do Not Buy Japanese Goods," the patriotic heart is bound to be aroused. This matter is small, but its impact is great. The amount of money collected and resolved by each store every day is not small, and the financial industry is the general exchange of currency. If the rubber stamp of "Do Not Buy Japanese Goods" is stamped on the banknotes and silver coins issued and received, it will be widely circulated and easily spread for the purpose of propaganda for economic severance with Japan. It is appropriate to send a letter to notify you and hope that your Association will forward it to your colleagues to follow suit.

Vietnamese Overseas Chinese Stop Distributing Japanese Goods

The Same Will Be Done in Seventeen Commercial Ports

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce received a letter from the Anti-Japanese Relief Association of Overseas Chinese in Central Vietnam yesterday, stating that since the Japanese pirates invaded my Southern Manchuria, after the news spread, all overseas Chinese were filled with indignation at the destruction of Japan. Amidst this excitement, the Anti-Japanese Relief Association of Overseas Chinese in Central Vietnam was organized to act as a backing for the negotiations between the motherland and Japan. Since Japan has always invaded my country with economic policies, it is necessary to boycott Japanese goods in order to control the Japanese slaves and benefit the livelihood of my country. Therefore, the second meeting of this association resolved to send a letter to the chambers of commerce of major commercial ports at home and abroad, and to notify the trade associations under their jurisdiction to stop distributing goods to the seventeen commercial ports under this association, in order to prevent the source of inferior goods. Anti-Japanese Work in All Sectors

Shops on Nanjing Road Welcome Inspection by the Municipal Federation: Zhang Yichen and others, members of the Shanghai Citizens' United Association's Committee for Inspecting Japanese Goods, together with committee members from the first district branch, began inspections and confiscations on Nanjing Road. They confiscated goods from watch shops such as Yi Tai Xiang, Shi Wei Ji, and Sino-American Watch Company, as well as Tian Lun Silk Shop and Quan Chang Xiang Foreign Goods Shop. They also filled out voluntary declarations stating they would never buy or sell Japanese goods, expressing their determination to sever economic ties with Japan. The various shops welcomed the inspection committee members of the Municipal Federation and willingly cooperated with the confiscations. It is reported that major companies such as Sincere, Wing On, and The Sun Sun, which were sealed by the first district branch of the Municipal Federation, are also willing to request the Municipal Federation to expedite further sealing to verify the situation.

The 17th District Branch of the Municipal Federation Began Inspections Yesterday: The 17th District Branch of the Citizens' United Association appointed Chen Jiufeng, Chen Xisheng, Fang Huijian, and Jiang Xianhe as members of the Committee for Inspecting Japanese Goods, and also invited Tan Yuchang, a specialist in foreign goods, Liu Taoru, a cotton cloth merchant, Gao Jieyuan, a seafood dealer, Shu Wenyao, a wood merchant, and committee members from the electrical materials industry. The entire committee went out yesterday to confiscate Japanese goods, including one small room with thirteen display windows at Tong Fa Xiang, one box at Yong Xiang, one box at Li Feng, one box at He Xing, one large display window at Zhao Ren Ji, fourteen pieces of glass and one other item at Tai Feng Store, one item at Xin Ru Bei Store, three items at Da Zhonghua, four boxes at the branch of Wuzhou Pharmacy, one box of Zhenhua crab meat, three items at Xin Yuan, one box of Wan Cheng seafood, one box of Tong Chang beer, four boxes of seafood at the Hongkou Restaurant, and six boxes at the Bailin Company.

Wing On Factory Workers Determined to Resist: The Workers' Economic Severance Association of the First Factory of Wing On Textile Company issued a declaration and regulations yesterday. The eighth article of the regulations is recorded as follows: (1) Members of this association must register all Japanese goods they possess after the establishment of this association. (2) After registration, members pledge not to purchase any more Japanese goods. (3) If there are domestic products that can replace any item, members must purchase domestic products. (4) If a member is unable to determine whether a necessary item is Japanese when purchasing it, they must first report to the standing executive committee of this association. They may only purchase the item after a clear investigation; otherwise, it will be considered a deliberate violation. (5) In addition to swearing to never buy Japanese goods themselves, members of this association must also monitor and persuade their relatives and friends. (6) If a member of this association discovers that another member has violated the regulations, they must immediately report it to the standing executive committee. Ninth article, penalties: (1) Those who violate the above regulations will be dealt with by a meeting of the standing executive committee. (2) In more serious cases, the executive committee may convene a general meeting of all members to deal with the matter. (3) Members of this association who discover that another member has purchased Japanese goods and conceals it will also be subject to punishment by the standing executive committee. (4) If there is clear and conclusive evidence of purchasing Japanese goods, the executive committee will decide, in the name of this association, to notify the member in writing of their dismissal and publicly announce the facts to show impartiality. (5) If, after being notified in the name of this association, the member relies on their power and refuses to leave, the colleagues of this association will not cooperate with them to show their determination to not be Chinese. Tenth article, supplementary provisions: These regulations shall take effect immediately upon approval by the founding congress on October 18, 1931.

Increased Coal Freight Rates on the Jiaoji Railway

Coal Industry Requests Assistance

The Japanese Director of the Railway Traffic Department

Takes the Opportunity to Periodically Increase Prices

Telegrams to the Central Government to Repeal the Increase

The Shanghai Coal Industry Association sent a telegram stating: To the Shanghai Special City Party Department, Shanghai Municipal Government, Social Affairs Bureau, Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee, Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and all industrial, commercial, agricultural, and academic groups in Shanghai: The invasion by the violent Japanese is causing indignation among people and gods. Severing economic ties with Japan is the duty of every citizen and a unanimous demand. Japanese coal, as a commodity, is naturally no exception. The southern provinces of China have historically consumed up to two-thirds of the total amount of Japanese coal. Now that it is being rejected, domestic coal should be urgently transported to replace it. If the transport of domestic coal is delayed, the southern provinces will immediately face a coal shortage. If coal runs out, the functions of warships, merchant ships, trains, and all factories, electric lights, and tap water will completely cease to operate. Such an environment is extremely dangerous. As of October 20, the total stock of coal in Shanghai is only 300,000 tons, which is only enough to supply for one month. Therefore, it is urgent to transport domestic coal to replenish the supply. However, the Japanese director of the Jiaoji Railway Traffic Department is taking this opportunity to periodically increase freight rates for domestic coal, effective November 1. The special export price has been increased from 2.52 yuan per ton to 2.80 yuan, leading to reports of Shandong mines suspending operations. Such actions are tantamount to harming our national lifeline. In addition to urgently telegraphing the central government to order the repeal, we hereby request assistance to cancel the increased freight rates for coal on the Jiaoji Railway to avoid a coal shortage. This matter concerns the national lifeline. We implore your approval and urgently submit this petition for your consideration. Shanghai Coal Industry Association.

Rectifying Tobacco and Alcohol Taxes and Implementing Registration

The National Government, in view of the consumption of tobacco and alcohol, plans to strictly prohibit them, but considering the difficulties of the industry, it will first register and rectify them to indicate that taxes are collected with tickets. The Ministry of Finance has now established the National Tobacco and Alcohol Merchants Registration Office next to the Popular Cinema on Zhonghua Road, Xiaonanmen. In addition to appointing Director Yin and Director Shen, there are also various staff members such as registration investigators, as well as tea servants and messengers, totaling more than 30 people. The entire Jiangsu Province is expected to be completed within six months.

Quarantine Office Reports on Cholera Prevention

The National Seaport Quarantine Office issued the thirteenth report on cholera prevention: (1) According to last week's report, Yu Wu claimed to have predicted that cholera could be alleviated. However, in the most recent week (ending October 17), there were 30 patients and 5 deaths, which is now being verified. The breakdown by jurisdiction is as follows: Shanghai City had 12 patients and 3 deaths, the Public Concession had 15 patients and 1 death, and the French Concession had 3 patients and 1 death. In total, there were 30 patients and 5 deaths. (2) Because there are still a few cases of cholera in Shanghai, the Shanghai Epidemic Hospital on Xizang Road is still receiving patients as usual. The hospital focuses on practical work, as always. (3) According to reports from Hankou and various flood-stricken areas, cholera has also decreased sharply, and the total number of patients is less than 1,000. From this, it can be seen that the Water Disaster Relief Committee has paid close attention to epidemic prevention work. (4) Various agencies in Shanghai Seaport stopped cholera prevention injections on October 7. From May 1, a total of 522,466 people were vaccinated. The French Concession stopped on October 15. From April 1, 63,874 people were vaccinated. The number of the Public Concession will be finalized and published next week. (5) The report on the plague in Henan was untrue, as previously reported by newspapers. This office sent many technicians to investigate, and the patients suffered from severe tertian malaria, not plague. The number of deaths was no more than 100. From this, it can be seen the importance of establishing health agencies in various provinces, so that the health reports can be used as a reference for countries around the world, so as not to be misleading. (6) As for the plague discovered between Shaanxi and Shanxi, it is definitely correct, because that place was the center of a local epidemic of plague ten years ago. The National Government is very concerned about this disaster and hopes to eliminate the most harmful plague as soon as possible. It has ordered the concentration of medical and health personnel to go to rescue, and the personnel of the Northeast Epidemic Prevention Office have also packed their bags and left Harbin to go to Taiyuan, and then to the disaster area to rescue.

Preparations for the National Anti-Drug Conference

Representatives are being recommended by overseas and domestic organizations

Concrete representations will be made to the government

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association originally scheduled to convene the National Anti-Drug Representatives Conference at the West Lake in Hangzhou on November 1. Subsequently, due to the invasion of the violent Japanese, the whole country unanimously confronted foreign countries, and the Conference decided to postpone the Conference to January 1 to 5 next year. Separate telegrams have been sent to anti-drug organizations in various places for reference. It is reported that remote associations such as the Singapore Anti-Drug Association have appointed the vice chairman of the association, Lin Jindian, to return to the country to attend. The Anti-Drug Association specifically telegraphed to invite him to postpone his visit to Hangzhou. In addition, Dr. Chen Jinhuang, a smoking cessation expert from the Batavia Anti-Drug Association, was also specially invited by the association to attend the meeting. Mr. Chen arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and led several well-known overseas Chinese doctors to Han first to assist in epidemic prevention in the disaster area. He will come to Hangzhou to attend the meeting at that time. In addition, dozens of anti-drug associations in Chengdu, Tianjin, Andong, Liaoning, Fuzhou, Xiamen, Kaifeng, Taiwan, Yancheng, Rugao, Wujin, Pei County, Yangzhong, Dongtai, Yutai, Zhao County, etc., have nominated representatives to register with the Conference Preparatory Office and submitted proposals, and the situation is very enthusiastic. In addition, Lu Zhengxiang, a member of the association, also sent a congratulatory message to the Conference from Belgium a few days ago and has high hopes for this Conference. Also, anti-drug organizations, women's organizations, and social movement leaders in England, the United States, France, Germany, the Netherlands, Switzerland, and Belgium are all preparing to express their cooperation with the people's groups of our country at this Conference. There have been many inquiries about the details of the Conference in recent days, and Blanc, the president of the International Anti-Drug Propaganda Society in Geneva, has even telegraphed to advocate that the Conference launch a movement to boycott narcotic drugs, imitating the method of boycotting Japanese goods, in order to use the sanctions of public opinion to achieve effective results. It is reported that the association believes that drug addiction is a fatal wound to our country and plans to make a detailed plan to submit to the Conference for thorough discussion. It is reported that this Conference will make a thorough and concrete representation to the government on the nationwide smoking ban based on the public opinion of the people of the whole country, and will request the government to guarantee that it will effectively stop the counter-propaganda and activities of those who advocate the opium public sale in order to prevent the recurrence of old evils.

Case of a Japanese Man Shooting and Injuring a Chinese Policeman

First Act of Trouble-Making by Dalian Rogues

The Municipal Government Lodged a Serious Protest

The Reversal of Truth by Japanese Newspapers and Propaganda

The details of the case in which Wang Changxing, a policeman of the Sixth Squad of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, was shot and injured by a Japanese man on Doule'an Road at 0:15 AM yesterday have been detailed in yesterday's newspaper. The Municipal Government believes that the Japanese arbitrarily shot and injured a policeman maintaining public order, which is an intentional act of provocation, and has lodged a serious protest with the Japanese Consulate. However, there are some details of the cause of this case that were not detailed in yesterday's newspaper, so they are supplemented as follows: At the time, the license plate number of the car carrying the Japanese was 12609, which belongs to the Zhongshan Automobile Company at 294 Zhapu Road. Beforehand, at around 11:40 PM, the Lion Hotel ordered a Chinese child to hire a car from the Zhongshan Automobile Company, driven by the driver Lu Peiwang, and drove to the hotel. At that time, three Japanese men got into the car, and another four people followed. Then, they ordered the driver to stop and wait, and the time was quite long. The driver told them that stopping for so long would cost more money, and the Japanese agreed. Later, all seven people got into the car and proceeded east on Doule'an Road and north on Doule'an Road. Then, they ordered the driver to turn back, three or four times, and their actions were very secretive. Finally, they drove to the parking lot next to the hut at the intersection of East Yokohama Road and stopped. The Japanese gave the driver a silver dollar and two jiao, and the driver was unhappy because it had been a long time and he had to add more. Unexpectedly, two Japanese men beat him. The driver ran wildly in pain to the post 30 meters away and reported to the policeman Wang Changshun. Wang then went with Lu. When several Japanese men saw the policeman coming, they suddenly stepped forward and surrounded him. One of them shot at Wang, and tried to seize the box cannon he was wearing. For self-defense, Wang also fired a shot. The Japanese started to be afraid to offend again. The gun fired by the Japanese assailant hit the center of Wang Changshun's left hand. The policeman was injured and returned to the Yokohama Bridge squad headquarters to report the emergency. At that time, it happened that Inspector Gao of the Fifth District and Chief Chen of the Police Station were patrolling here and were also violently beaten by the Japanese. The nearby Japanese Marine Corps headquarters had already sent a large number of armed Japanese soldiers to the scene to demonstrate. Soon, the Western Detective of the Disweilu Police Station heard the news and rushed to the scene. He found a blank hand-gun cartridge case on the ground, which was obviously fired by the Japanese. Because what Wang Changshun was wearing was a box cannon, the cartridge case was completely different. One of the Japanese perpetrators, Nishimura Chihiro, Matsumoto Koji, and another Taiwanese, Huang Kuanju, were arrested by the police and detained for interrogation. However, the wounds on the palm of the Japanese Matsumoto were scratches from the ground, not bullet wounds. After this incident, the residents in the vicinity were very panic-stricken and guessed that these troublemaking Japanese must be rogues who had just come to Shanghai from Dalian. Their organization is in teams of four or five people, carrying pistols, specializing in making trouble for the Chinese. Once an incident occurs, the Japanese Navy can make a big deal out of it, reverse black and white, and create a serious situation in order to carry out their poisonous plan of sabotage. Moreover, the location of the incident, at the intersection of Doule'an Road and East Yokohama Road, is very close to the Japanese Naval Marine Corps headquarters, and their deliberate sabotage is even more obvious. Also, according to another report, the details of the case of the Japanese shooting and injuring a policeman of the Public Security Bureau on East Yokohama Road have been described above. However, regarding the circumstances of the cause of this case, the local Japanese newspapers unanimously made a reversal propaganda report, obliterating the facts and trying to confuse public opinion. They insisted that the Japanese did not carry guns, that the policeman shot himself, and that the Brown Ning cartridge case found at the scene was used by the policeman. The viciousness of their framing and biting back is truly appalling. When the incident occurred, there was only one policeman, Wang Changshun, at the post. According to the regulations of the Public Security Bureau, the guns carried by the patrols are either rifles or box guns, and the patrol chiefs and above wear pistols. Since Wang Changshun is a patrol, he would naturally wear a box gun. Since there were no other police officers next to Wang, the Brown Ning cartridge case found on the ground was undoubtedly used by the Japanese. The Japanese newspaper also said that the cartridge case was put there by the police, which is unfounded and even more absurd.

Second Day of the Pacific Conference of Learning

Chinese Economic Issues to be Discussed in Three Days

Yesterday's Special Discussion on the Development of Agriculture

Shen Shi Telegraphic News Agency reported that yesterday was the second day of the Pacific International Learning Association conference. Before 9:00 AM, committee members from various countries had arrived at the site one after another. At 9:00 AM, the roundtable meeting began, still divided into four groups for discussion, titled "Economic Development of China." The discussion ended at nearly 10:00 AM. After a short break, the meeting continued at 11:15 AM. The groups held joint discussions, and Xia Pingfang, director of the Trust Department of the Bank of China, gave a speech on behalf of Zhang Gongquan on Chinese financial issues, and Herbert, a foreign affairs consultant of HSBC, gave a speech on foreign investment in China. At 12:15 PM, the Agenda Committee and the Chairman's Secretary held a joint meeting. At 12:45 PM, the Chinese Committee hosted a public banquet for all the committee members. From 8:30 PM to 9:15 PM, Dr. Xia Jinlin gave a speech. From 10:00 PM to 10:50 PM, the Agenda Committee held a meeting. The discussion on the economic development of China is summarized as follows.

Economic Development in China

Divided into Three Days for Discussion: Yesterday was the First Day, Dedicated to Discussing Agricultural Development. A Chairman of one group, during the roundtable meeting, stated that Greek civilization was based on slavery, modern European and American civilization on machinery, while Chinese civilization is based on agriculture. The area of land cultivated by Chinese people is particularly small; those exceeding fifteen acres account for only six percent, with one-third cultivating less than one acre. Furthermore, manual labor is used for cultivation, with the hope of producing food and fuel for farmers' own use. Chinese farmers account for about eighty percent of the population, and transportation across the country is mostly inconvenient. The diligence and efficiency of Chinese farmers are derived from customs and experience, and they lack modern scientific methods. Yesterday's roundtable meeting focused on agricultural education and research, and how to implement these in the actual lives of farmers. It was generally agreed that agricultural education in China is still in its infancy, but the agricultural schools established in several places in Central China, South China, and North China have achieved remarkable results. Privately established institutions are also commendable. However, to gain the trust of farmers, great skill and ingenuity are required to make them understand that the improvement of seeds, the prevention of pests, etc., are all for their benefit, and not for the self-interest of the instructors. The first step is to establish small-scale rural lending programs, providing low-interest loans to farmers, and giving them improved seeds. In their vicinity, widespread experiments should be conducted on improved planting methods, so that farmers can witness the results and emulate them. It was generally agreed that foreigners can currently assist in higher education and research, without any objection. However, the practical work must be done by the Chinese themselves. For example, Japan does not have a good agricultural experiment station in Manchuria, yet its agricultural methods still cannot influence the thirty million Chinese farmers in Manchuria. A Chinese representative said, "I am still unaware of what influence the ninety-three Japanese farmers in Manchuria have had." A Japanese representative said that Japanese people in Manchuria hardly engage in farming because Japanese people cannot compete with Chinese farmers using their own methods. Japanese emigrants in America who have learned American planting methods are now restricted by American laws and cannot apply them in America, but they can still apply them in Manchuria and compete with Chinese farmers. The interest rates for loans for Chinese farmers are very high, about 2.5% to 3% in Central China, and as high as 4% in the three northeastern provinces. In the interior, borrowing and repayment without using money can even double the interest. Therefore, establishing a rural lending system to provide low-interest loans to farmers is a necessary step in promoting agriculture. If farmers do not have funds for assistance, then knowledge of seed selection and fertilization is entirely useless. The development of rural lending in Japan was presented in an interesting way during the discussion. In the Tokugawa era, rural lending groups were formed to lend to those who bid the highest interest rate. In the Meiji era, more than fifty years ago, rural lending institutions and cooperatives were established, modeled after the German system, providing farmers with access to ordinary capital, and applying capital used for urban industry and commerce to agriculture. The tasks of these lending institutions were, first, to advance loans to farmers; and second, to cooperatively purchase supplies, sell agricultural products, and jointly rent or purchase machinery, etc. However, whether Japanese agriculture has reached the second stage is questionable. Members cannot be without funds, and the capitalist system applied to urban industry and commerce is promoted because it can provide valuable social services, thus benefiting the system. However, applying this to agriculture will be counterproductive. Farmers produce food for people, and the greater their social service, the more disadvantageous it is for themselves. The path to prosperity seems to lie in reducing this kind of service. There is currently a movement, not towards communism, but towards a cooperative form similar to Guild Socialism, which is particularly evident in Japan. Observers from the United States and Canada have also expressed doubts about whether efforts should be made to increase agricultural production at present. The issue of utilizing mountainous areas was also discussed. The majority of the Chinese representatives believed that there would probably not be much progress at present.

Because farmers must produce their own food and fuel, the greatest utilization of these mountainous areas lies in producing fuel. Utilizing the land on the mountain sides to plant fruit trees, raise silkworms, and extract silk has also seen some development, especially the tussah silk produced in Shandong Province, which comes from oak trees. Regarding the reorganization of land into sections to facilitate the use of machinery, it is currently not feasible. Chinese farmland is suffering from an excess of labor, so there is no need for labor-saving machinery in farming. However, simple water pumps for irrigation, and harvesting machines, etc., can be used cooperatively. The greatest uneconomical aspect of dividing land into sections is the excessive time wasted traveling from field A to field B. The comprehensive study of irrigation, forest cultivation, and flood control was also briefly discussed. One group also discussed transportation, such as the development of railways, the need for highways, and the adoption of a type of automobile transport that travels slower and is cheaper than standard commercial vehicles, and is more suitable for bad roads.

Tearing Up a Page of Accounts to Conceal Evidence of Marriage

Yu Qiusheng's Bigamy Trial Continues

Western Detective Discovers New Evidence

Yu Qiusheng, the owner of the Da De Rubber Factory, falsely claimed that his first wife was dead and colluded with his friend Xu Kuiqing to deceive Wang Pan, a seventeen-year-old woman from Shaoxing, into becoming his concubine under the guise of taking a second wife. After a month, Wang Pan prepared gifts to visit this promising son-in-law, and the matter was exposed. She immediately took her daughter back and reported it to the police, who filed a bigamy lawsuit against Yu. However, Yu dared to defy the law and had Xu Kuiqing and Li Yunbao, an employee of the New World Hotel, which was rented as the wedding hall on the day of the marriage, give false statements to the First Special District Court during the trial, denying that a grand ceremony was held to help Yu deny the charges. Judge Feng saw through their lies and ordered Yu Qiusheng to be released on bail after paying 2,000 yuan. Xu and Li were also each ordered to post bail and await investigation. The details have been repeatedly recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng continued the trial. The two lawyers representing the defendant Yu Qiusheng both found it inconvenient to continue representing Yu due to certain issues. Therefore, Yu has hired another lawyer, Wang, to appear in court to defend him. However, many of the key witnesses who were summoned did not arrive yesterday, and Xu Kuiqing also claimed to be ill and did not appear. First, Wang Pan, the mother of the plaintiff Wang Qiaoxian, described the defendant's deception, saying that Yu Qiusheng first saw her daughter at the home of a neighbor surnamed Chen in May of the lunar calendar and then conceived the idea of marrying her. He then came to her house three or four times, claiming that his wife had passed away and that he wanted to marry her daughter as a replacement. He then asked Xu Kuiqing to act as a matchmaker and set the engagement gift at 520 yuan, including 200 yuan for clothing and accessories, 200 yuan for dowry, and 120 yuan for wedding cakes. She then ordered her eldest son-in-law, Feng Bolin, to act as a matchmaker for her daughter. On the fifth day of the sixth lunar month, a red invitation was sent, and she received one of them and returned the rest. She did not pay attention to the wording of the invitation at first, so she did not read it carefully. On the ninth day of the sixth lunar month (i.e., July 23), the Yu family used a wedding car to lead a band to the Hongxiang Hotel, which she had rented as a wedding hall, to pick up the bride's auspicious attire. The wedding attire was also brought by Xu Kuiqing. The wedding hall was rented at the New World Hotel. Feng Bolin was invited to attend the ceremony. She had originally planned to return to her parents' home on the same day, but Yu firmly declined, saying that he was too busy. Therefore, she did not hold a banquet on that day and instead arranged a banquet at the Tongxing Restaurant on August 2 to invite the groom and bride to dine together and meet with relatives. However, only Yu arrived at that time, saying that the bride was sick and could not come. When she visited her son-in-law after a month, she first went to Tongdeli in the French Concession and then learned that he had moved to Zhangchuan Lane in the city. After being guided by someone, her daughter told her the whole story. She immediately questioned Qiusheng, saying, "You said your wife was dead, but why do you still have a wife? Aren't you treating my daughter as a concubine?" Qiusheng then said that she was indeed being treated as a concubine, and his tone was extremely arrogant. He also said that the matter was already done, and she could do whatever she wanted. She felt that she was being insulted too much, so she took her daughter and filed a lawsuit. Then, Western Detective Laomen of the Xinzha Police Station reported the situation of retrieving the account books at the New World Hotel, saying that in addition to the account books in the case, there was also another book. According to the manager of the hotel, surnamed Zhou, Yu Qiusheng borrowed it earlier to copy down the types of expenses on that day. However, when he returned it, he tore out a page recording that item of account. Therefore, this account book has been hidden by the general manager in an iron box for further negotiation with Yu. Zhou also said that his cousin would send the account book to the case, but Zhou has not been seen today and is presumed to be ill. At that time, the police chief's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, also submitted the account books opened by the Hongxiang Hotel to the case, saying that someone from the hotel had testified earlier, firmly claiming that the bride's family did not put up lanterns and decorations, but now, upon reading the hotel's bill, there are expenses for such items, so the hotel is also suspected of perjury. Judge Feng then examined the account books of the New World Hotel one by one. The defendant's rental of the hotel's wedding hall was on July 23, but the account items recorded in the account books were on July 26. This item of account is clearly inconsistent with Yu's account. Therefore, he asked Yu about the tearing up of the account book. Yu claimed that what he borrowed was the tea servant's record and not a ledger. The Western detective then reaffirmed that, according to Zhou's statement, it was indeed a formal account book. Later, Judge Feng adjourned the hearing to the morning of the 29th of this month because several key witnesses had not arrived, and ordered the summons of witnesses to continue the trial.

Security Chief Interferes in Judicial Police

Recaptures Arrested Criminal

Court Imposes Strict Sanctions

In Longwang Temple, Pudong, an elderly woman named Fu Xiao had a daughter named Jin Ying. Last year, she recruited Fu Zhangjian as her son-in-law. Unexpectedly, her nephews in the same clan, Fu Meisheng and Fu Shunsheng, coveted her property. After several quarrels, Fu Xiao made Fu Shunsheng her adopted son and divided the property equally between her daughter and adopted son. Unexpectedly, Fu Meisheng was dissatisfied because he did not get anything. In July of this year, he beat Fu Xiao, Fu Zhangjian, and Fu Jin Ying, etc. Fu Xiao, etc., filed a complaint with the local court, and after being ordered to summon them three times, the defendants refused to appear. Therefore, an arrest warrant was issued, ordering the bailiff Zhang Cheng to go and arrest them. When he went to the location yesterday morning, the plaintiff reported that Fu Meisheng was gambling in a teahouse. The police immediately went to arrest him. However, next to the teahouse was the Security Corps, and the chief, Luo Weiren, led more than ten people to seize Fu Meisheng and drag the bailiff away. Luo Weiren told him that the address written on the arrest warrant was Yanjiaqiao, and Longwang Temple was under his jurisdiction and could not be taken away. Otherwise, he would not be able to leave either. He then presented three silver dollars and asked him to take them quickly and leave quickly. If he needed anyone in the future, he should come to him. Seeing that he was outnumbered, the bailiff refused the silver dollars and refused to take the person away. Luo firmly put the silver dollars in the bailiff's clothing, threatening that if he did not take the money, he would not let him leave, etc., in order to prevent the bailiff from arresting people again in the future. The bailiff then asked for a business card and immediately returned to the court to report. After Chief Prosecutor Liu read the report, he was furious, saying that the Security Corps is a people's self-defense organization, and its duties are limited to protecting the local area and preventing bandits. It has no right to detain people. Now, it is interfering in the exercise of judicial power and seeking bribes with a mere Security Corps. What will happen to other administrative organs? If strict sanctions are not imposed, it will not be enough to maintain the prestige of the judiciary. Therefore, he immediately ordered the original handling prosecutor Wang to issue an arrest warrant, ordering police chief Xu Jinqing to supervise the bailiffs Xu Guoguang, Zhou Qiwen, Xue Bingzhang, Huang Hanqing, Zhu Baochang, Zhu Wanyuan, Zhang Chunshen, and Zhang Cheng, etc., to go to Pudong in full uniform and take Luo Weiren, Fu Meisheng, Fu Shunsheng, etc., back to the court for legal action.

China Merchants Bureau Thoroughly Investigates Workers Destroying the Inspection Office

The Jinliyuan Wharf of the China Merchants Bureau has an inspection office, which is responsible for wharf patrols, etc. The other day, the Bureau's Xinming ship arrived in Shanghai, and several coolies stole goods and were seized by the inspection office, which aroused the anger of the workers and destroyed the inspection office. The details of this incident are recorded below:

Theft Uncovered: The China Merchants Bureau's Beiyang ship Xinming arrived in Shanghai this time from Tianjin. While unloading the goods at Jinliyuan Wharf, three coolies stole goods such as tickets and hairy clams from the cabin of the Xinming ship. Taking advantage of the chaos of the coolies loading and unloading, they secretly hid the stolen goods, but were seen by the patrolmen of the South Wharf Inspection Office, who immediately arrested the three coolies and took them to the inspection office to await verification.

Workers Demand Release: After the three coolies who stole the goods were arrested by the patrolmen of the inspection office, the workers went to the inspection office in groups and demanded that the three workers be released immediately. The inspection office did not allow it, and more and more workers gathered in front of the door. Inspection director Zhu Gongshang reported to the head office on the one hand and went out to persuade the workers on the other hand, but to no avail.

Destruction of Objects: Because the workers' demands were ineffective, they used barbaric means and rushed into the inspection office, smashing everything they saw. All the desks and public objects in the office were destroyed. Seeing that the situation was bad, the staff temporarily avoided being injured.

Page 12

Release of Workers: During the chaos, the unloading of the Xinming ship had stopped, and at the same time, it incited the Xinjiangtian ship to stop working as well. The two ships could not load or unload goods. Later, the bureau sent someone to arrive and earnestly persuade the workers, promising to release the three workers on bail and ordering them to resume work immediately so as not to hinder navigation. The matter came to an end from 11:00 a.m. to 3:00 p.m. The workers, having achieved their goal, began to work.

Bureau Investigates: Guo Waifeng, general manager of the China Merchants Bureau, specially appointed Ye Chuanfang, deputy manager of operations, to thoroughly investigate this case and report it before verifying it. Yesterday, the inspection office had already repaired and rearranged the damaged objects in the office to facilitate office work. The outcome of this matter will be reported in the future.

Statement Regarding Potato Starch Mistakenly Identified as Japanese Goods

More than 3,000 pieces of potato starch from Yuanlaihang were identified by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association as Japanese goods and were resolved to be confiscated by the sixth executive committee meeting and reported to the municipal party headquarters for review. The company claimed that the potato starch was not Japanese goods and collected various conclusive evidence to apply for reconsideration by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. Wu Hankang, the manager of the company, also presented a statement to the municipal party headquarters, stating that the potato starch was not Japanese goods and was mistakenly detained and confiscated. He respectfully requested review of the matter. The merchant's Yuanlaihang, which he manages, specializes in selling goods from various islands in the South Seas, and also acts as an agent for overseas Chinese to buy and sell, and has been trading directly with Dutch, German, American, British, and Austrian companies for many years. It has never sold Japanese goods. Since June 19 of the Republic of China, it has successively ordered Dutch potato starch, also known as raw starch, from factories in Hamburg and Berlin, Germany, and transported it to Shanghai for sale many times. Before August 13 and 15 of this year, the inspection section of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Committee mistakenly identified the company's potato starch as Japanese goods and successively seized 3,346 pieces at Lujia Ferry and Yuanlai Warehouse, etc. Evidence was presented at the time to explain, and some understanding was gained. On September 3, a notice was received that the eighth executive committee meeting resolved that the goods were Dutch goods masquerading as Japanese goods and should be fined 3,000 yuan to help disaster relief, and the goods should be returned, etc. In order to quickly settle the matter, the merchant paid the amount in full and obtained a receipt dated September 4 and a notice of release. All matters have been concluded, but when going to the inspection section warehouse to collect the goods, the section delayed issuing the bill of lading. After repeated urging, it was ineffective and the goods were never returned. On the 16th of this month, it was suddenly seen in Shen Xin and other newspapers that the sixth executive committee meeting of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association had resolved to confiscate all of the above-mentioned potato starch, which was very frightening. The merchant's patriotism has never dared to lag behind others. If goods that are not Japanese goods are mistakenly identified as Japanese goods, they should be declared first. If they are resolved to be confiscated again, the economic loss is great, and the loss of reputation is huge. He immediately collected various conclusive evidence, prepared to request reconsideration, and first sent a letter to the association stating the matter. Upon seeing the report yesterday, he respectfully submitted a statement to the department, requesting an inspection. All reasons and evidence for requesting reconsideration, etc., will be submitted again later, combined with this statement.

Approved at Seven Li Per Fen by a Provincial Order. The Shanghai County Finance Bureau announced yesterday that, according to the records of the Nianfen rush grain tax to be collected in the county, the autumn harvest was poor. After the districts reported to the county, the commissioners of the Civil Affairs, Finance, Agriculture, and Mining Departments were ordered to go to the county to inspect the four villages in detail and calculate the amount of tax reduction. The previous request to reduce one fen was not approved. Therefore, the department tentatively decided to increase the levy by three li, changing it to a general reduction of seven li, with an actual levy of nine fen and three li. This is the final decision and no further objections may be raised. You should immediately follow these instructions, create a table of registration and send it for verification, without delay, etc. Upon receiving this order, we should follow the instructions and handle it. All busy taxes that were collected earlier in the year, and busy silver that was completed in tax reduction, should be deducted in the amount that rush silver will be completed next year and offset against the new tax. This announcement should be posted so that all business owners will be notified. This is the announcement.

Selling Alleged Antidotes Under False Pretenses

Health Bureau Alerts Citizens

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau issued a notice stating: It has been reported that recently some individuals have been peddling alleged antidotes to citizens, falsely claiming that due to the floods in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, the bureau, concerned about the pollution of the city's water source, has specially manufactured these antidotes for sale to citizens to dissolve in the water to prevent infection, etc. However, this bureau has not manufactured or sold any medications. This is clearly a fraudulent scheme by unscrupulous individuals to swindle money. Should such false representations be encountered in the future, citizens are urged to immediately report them to the police on duty, who will detain the suspects at the local precinct, and to also report to this bureau for thorough investigation. Furthermore, this bureau has always emphasized integrity in handling all health-related matters. If anyone attempts to extort money under any pretext, they can be reported with confidence, and we will conduct a fair investigation without any leniency. However, all businesses should also proactively focus on public health to prevent unscrupulous individuals from taking advantage of opportunities for extortion. Moreover, this bureau has not dispatched anyone to solicit donations. Any request for money under any pretext is also a fraudulent act and should be reported immediately for investigation. It is hoped that everyone will pay close attention to these matters.

Soviet Kerosene Dumping in China

Talk by Mr. Libanov, General Manager of the Trust

Content of the Contract Signed with Guanghua Company

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, the Soviet Russian Kerosene Trust is dumping kerosene in China, starting operations first in Shanghai, and has repeatedly consulted with Guanghua Kerosene Company, etc., as reported in various newspapers. Yesterday, a reporter from this agency interviewed Mr. Libanov, General Manager of the Trust, to inquire about the details. Mr. Libanov answered as follows:

Guanghua Kerosene Company is a limited liability company organized by Chinese merchants. The company is well-managed and enjoys a high reputation. I have come to your country as a representative of this Trust to sign a contract with the company to promote and sell kerosene in China. It is the only kerosene company in China whose managers possess commercial talent and have considerable experience in promoting kerosene. They have agencies throughout China and should have no problem selling 1.5 million gallons of kerosene per month. The company has a kerosene processing plant in Shanghai, which is very well-equipped, with several oil storage tanks and various modern machines, providing everything needed for the oil business. Soviet kerosene production is abundant, ranking third among oil-producing countries in the world. However, recently, other oil-producing countries have been affected by unstable economic conditions, resulting in reduced oil production. Therefore, the Soviet Union has become the second largest oil-producing country in the world in recent years. The current kerosene production of the Soviet Union is actually two and a half times more than the record before the Russian war. The Trust's original five-year oil industry plan can now be fully achieved in two and a half years, based on the actual work in the first half of this year, instead of five years. The so-called five-year plan means intensifying work to double the annual kerosene production to 46 million tons by the end of the fifth year. With the increase in Soviet kerosene production, the number of kerosene exports will certainly increase accordingly. In 1929-1930, the Soviet Union exported 4.62 million tons of kerosene, which is about five times higher than the highest number before the Russian war. Soviet kerosene is not only selling well in the United States but is also popular all over the world. I (Mr. Libanov) am now indicating the amount of kerosene produced in the Soviet Union so that it is clear that there is no difficulty for the Soviet Union to supply a portion of the needs of the Chinese market. China's annual consumption of various kerosene oils is only 1 million tons. The contract signed between this Trust and Guanghua Company states that the General Manager of Guanghua Company will promote and sell kerosene from the Soviet Kerosene Trust in fifteen provinces in China. The contract is for a period of five years. After the various sales matters are completed, the Guanghua Kerosene Company will begin sales. They have already placed an order with this Trust for a batch of kerosene. The goods will be transported and sold to various places by Guanghua Company. The oil tanker "Owen" is loaded with 3.1 million gallons of kerosene. The oil was loaded at the port of Poti (transliteration) in the Black Sea on September 22, passing through the four port (transliteration). The entire journey takes 33 days and will arrive in Shanghai on the 25th of this month. According to the contract, all kerosene sold will be transported from the Black Sea by several oil tankers through the Don River (transliteration) to Shanghai. The reporter further asked whether Guanghua Company would be the exclusive agent for all kinds of oil products from the Soviet Union in the future. Mr. Libanov replied that the contract signed with Guanghua Company states that it will only manage kerosene in the fifteen provinces south of the Yellow River in China. Guanghua Company can sell all kinds of oils such as car oil, machine oil, and diesel oil throughout China, but this condition is not stated in the contract, and the Trust has full authority to negotiate other sales methods with other Chinese merchants. The reporter also asked what rules and regulations the Soviet kerosene would adopt when it is sold in China in the future, and whether it would affect the business of other kerosene experts in the world. Mr. Libanov replied that the Soviet Union will adopt independent rules and regulations when selling kerosene in China. In order to protect their own positions, kerosene producers in the world must have considerable considerations. However, the future activities of the Soviet Kerosene Trust will be carried out in accordance with the appropriate business methods already used by other companies. They will never use the method of price competition to suppress the sales of other companies. If price competition occurs, all kerosene experts will not benefit from it. I firmly believe that this kind of activity will not occur. If the Soviet Kerosene Trust is excluded and cannot gain a foothold in China, the Soviet Union will certainly have considerable ability to resist such disputes. All organizations in China will not retreat. Because the kerosene produced in the Soviet Union is of high quality and the price is equal to other companies, I firmly believe that it will sell well in the market. Otherwise, how could the Soviet kerosene, which was transported by the American kerosene company and sold by Guanghua Company, gain a foothold in China?

Reader's Letter

Respectfully Informing All Yarn Factories in the Country about the Yarn Industry Shaochang

(The item of boycotting cotton yarn is enough to control Japan's fate. I hope that Chinese merchants will expand their equipment with the huge profits gained from boycotting Japan, so that supply and demand can match, and workers who leave Japanese factories can be employed and benefit more.)

Since the violent Japanese invasion of our Eastern Provinces, public sentiment has been indignant, and the call to resist Japanese goods has been widespread. This is the ninth boycott of Japanese goods since the establishment of the Republic of China. Looking back on the past, every one of them started with excitement and generosity, but ended with disappearance and silence. Speaking of our yarn industry, we have many more feelings about this, because Japanese goods coming to China, cotton yarn is the most important, and it is also an indispensable item for the lives of compatriots across the country. If everything is boycotted, and cotton yarn is not boycotted, then it is equivalent to not boycotting other things. If none of the other things are boycotted, and only the item of cotton yarn can make Japanese products disappear in our Chinese land, then it can make the three islands of Japan stagnate in production, increase unemployment, and cause economic depression. If our country persists in this way, and controls its fate, then the crisis in the Eastern Provinces can be resolved, and the alliance under the city can be avoided. It is a pity that it is still too early to say this today. Although the domestic yarn industry in our country has developed rapidly in recent years, it still cannot compete with Japanese commercial yarn sellers for even a single day. The quality cannot compete with imported goods, and the supply and demand are disparate. The output of the factory cannot satisfy the needs of the whole country. In addition, the factory management is not in place, and there is no research on business aspects. Even commercial ethics are weak, and they do not care about the overall situation of the country, the future of the industry, or even take it into account. I am saying this for the sake of my colleagues, and I am truly sighing. If the supply is insufficient to meet the demand, and this is also a daily necessity, then how can the boycott be sustained? Therefore, those who destroy the anti-Japanese resistance are not necessarily the merchants and profiteers who are blinded by profit, but are also forced by the situation and cannot avoid it. Since the Fresh Case occurred, the people's anger has been tense, and Japanese yarn has been rejected by our people. Therefore, the sales of Chinese yarn have shown a vigorous trend again. All gangs compete to advance, and even tens of thousands of packages of ten-strand yarn have been depleted. The price of yarn has risen sharply, while the price of raw cotton has fallen, and the cost is lighter. The profits are so great that they have not been seen in recent years. The Japanese merchants and yarn factories have taken advantage of the opportunity to dump a large batch of 70,000 to 80,000 packages at a price of more than 20 taels lower than Chinese yarn per package. However, although Japanese yarn is more than 20 taels lower than Chinese yarn, it still has a surplus of more than 10 taels in terms of cost. Then the profits of Chinese yarn are knowable. Recently, I read the letter from the United Association of Chinese Yarn Factories to the Anti-Japanese and National Salvation Association, stating that the price of Chinese yarn will not rise due to the boycott of Japanese goods. I am somewhat confused about this. The price of goods fluctuates due to supply and demand, which is known to everyone. If in normal times, the demand exceeds the supply, then we cannot criticize the increase in the price of goods. This is a special time, which is related to the national economy and the people's livelihood of our country, and it is also the key to the success or failure of this anti-Japanese resistance. Since the price of Chinese yarn is higher than that of Japanese yarn, even if the price is not increased now, has the function of pooling wisdom and efforts to the utmost been fulfilled? Or is there anything more? Wealthy merchants and officials, whose pockets are filled with money, are all wearing wool, serge, or domestically produced silk. In fact, most of my poor compatriots wear cloth clothes. If the cheap Japanese yarn disappears, and the expensive Chinese yarn does not reduce the price, then my poor civilians will not suffer from the burden of rising cloth prices, and those who get huge profits are not enjoying the benefits of the anti-Japanese movement? In other words, are they not taking advantage of the national misfortune to gain blessings? For the sake of the national situation, the livelihood of the civilians, and the business itself, it is better to use this huge and accidental profit to expand internal capital, or add spinning machines, or set up factories, so that supply and demand can match, the profits are greater, and the patriotic workers who leave the Japanese factories can also have a place to be employed. This is a win-win plan. I hope that Chinese yarn factories can implement it. After the Fresh Case, the anti-Japanese atmosphere was not vigorous for a while, but if there had been no Shenyang Incident, then the energy could be exhausted within ten days, and the previous anti-Japanese movement would become a fleeting bubble. It was not until the violent Japanese occupied my territory, massacred my people, and burned my houses that they knew that the disaster of national subjugation was imminent. Therefore, those colleagues who used to specialize in Japanese yarn knew fear and could also endure the pain to sacrifice in the hope of gathering the public's will to become a city and saving the country with conscience. Now try to ask anyone in the market about the yarn industry after the boycott, and they will definitely sigh and lament that they will be in panic of being unemployed, because the productive capacity of my country's yarn factories is too weak. If the factories that are making huge profits now do not urgently plan to expand, and the capitalists outside the industry have no intention of investing, then those who are now sacrificing in the yarn industry will have the worry of running out of food, and the future of the boycott will be even more hopeless.

The reply letters were sent to the address in the letter, but they were returned by the post office. It is said that there is no information to be found. I hope you will show a correct and detailed address again, and attach a considerable amount of postage stamps, so that I can send them to you. Thank you.

Free Talk

The Sound of Anti-Japanese Resistance

— Rui Hongchu

Parents beat their children, and the children offer themselves to the whip. This is called filial piety. Older brothers reprimand younger siblings, and the younger siblings humbly accept the training. This is called respect. Now, Japan is invading our Northeast, slaughtering our soldiers and civilians, and our country is responding with non-resistance. I wonder what this is called. The fields of the Northeast do not need fertilizer for cultivation. The soybeans of the Northeast can be considered the best in the world. (Nearly five hundred varieties) The forests and minerals are sufficient to meet the needs of the whole country for hundreds of years. If Japan had not invaded, how would those of us who have no money to study, and those who study only for love, know this kind of wisdom about the Northeast?

Foreigners ridicule us for having only five minutes of enthusiasm. If foreigners are referring to one person, then we have 200 million minutes when calculated by 400 million people. More than 33.333 million hours can be heated up in order, which is quite self-satisfied.

Remove the weeds in the courtyard, Zhai Futan Hui

The Last Scene of a Good Government

In 1922, Hu Shi drafted a "Our Political Propositions" and published it. The names listed included Wang Chonghui, Cai Yuanpei, Luo Wengan, and Hu Shi himself, totaling sixteen people. In this manifesto, they advocated establishing a government. The political reforms of a good government include three basic principles: first, a constitutional government; second, an open government; and third, a planned political system. Later, Wang Chonghui had a successful career and actually became the Premier, and Luo Wengan also became the Minister of Finance. At this time, the good people thought that the time was ripe to implement their own propositions. Everyone organized a political discussion meeting, which was held every Friday. After several meetings, Premier Wang always refused to announce his major policies, which made everyone very impatient. Once I went to Beijing, and it happened to be Friday, so my friends pulled me to participate in the discussion. My record is:

"Cai Yuanpei" Chairman

Hu Shi stood up:

"Based on our political propositions, we want to ask Premier Wang to announce his major policies and plans."

Wang Chonghui went on stage and said a bunch of rambling complaints for a full hour. Finally, he said in a particularly loud voice:

"Hu Shi! You want me to announce a plan, I have no plan! No plan is my plan..."

Cai Yuanpei: "This discussion of ours was originally set up for exchanging knowledge. Now, such a quarrel will only hurt feelings. It's better not to hold it. If everyone agrees, we will adjourn this meeting from now on."

Everyone agreed with Cai's proposal, and the play of the "good government" closed from then on.

Wu Tingfang and Ito Hirobumi

— Huang Yingdai

Japan is able to be so ferocious and so strong. Of course, it must be attributed to the Meiji Restoration. Looking back, although China was poor and weak fifty years ago, it was fully exposed. But compared with Japan, it was even more so. However, after only ten years, my great China was defeated by the Japanese. The reason for this is that after the Japanese Restoration, people were employed properly. The Chinese Qing government could not employ talents. At that time, there was no lack of talent in China. However, the students who studied in the West were often envied in the officialdom after returning to China and could not be employed. It is said that at that time, there was a student studying abroad who worked under Li Hongzhang. His monthly salary was only seven taels of silver.

Going to National Crisis

— He Tianjian

Alas, the fate of the country is now at this point. I only feel that the day is coming to an end. The country is full of tears. When I get up and look around, I am glad that the hearts of the people are not dead. There is an ancient saying that sorrow can rejuvenate the country. The people of the country can unite against the outside world. Even if the violent sun is savage, it is not enough to worry about. Every time I read Yue Wumu's "Man Jiang Hong" lyrics, I have the thought of reining in my horse at Guanshan and swinging my knife across the world. Because I feel that the lyrics are difficult to understand, but the feeling is really deep. So I wrote this song. It's time to go to the national crisis. There is power to help with power, and there is money to help with money. Working hard to stay as a slave is better than fighting with the enemy to decide who is the hero. Sitting and waiting for people to confiscate the property is better than being selfless and forgetting private interests. The Northeast has been looted, and the Central Plains are spreading again. Like carp, warships are coming endlessly, and the ports of the rivers and seas are in danger again. The League of Nations and the Non-War Treaty, paper tigers are not enough to look forward to. Justice has been lost for a long time. Where can we know right and wrong? The country and the nation are originally supported by strong forces. Strengthen their wisdom. The fate of prosperity and decline is in the hands of learning. Strengthen their courage. The luck of prosperity and decline is supported by force. Reading the Book of Filial Piety when disaster is imminent. Who can understand the words? It's time to go to the national crisis.

Don't hesitate to go to the national crisis. Endure my divine descendants to be humiliated by those snakes and insects. Tian Heng has righteous men. He would rather sacrifice on the island than submit. Gou Jian suffered his ambition. Poor pawns were destroyed. This heart is not a mat of straw. Don't be suspicious when the opportunity comes. Some say that the ignorant people forget the country but not the wealth. With wealth, the family can go to all countries. Ning is suffering from the disaster of one country. Some say that the ignorant people falsely recognize a hill of moss. China and Japan are the same race. It doesn't matter if he comes. What day is today? How can we blame each other? The people of the country are all wise. There is no such idiocy. I believe that 400 million people have the same hatred and do not know shame. The enemy is already in front of you. You are still mocking yourself. These people have been dead for a long time. It is really sad to say. Don't hesitate to go to the national crisis.

Silver. In the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895, China was defeated. Li Hongzhang was sent to Japan to negotiate the Treaty of Shimonoseki. Li Hongzhang was very surprised to see the development of Japanese industry and the wealth of the military. At the meeting, he asked Ito why Japan's progress was so rapid and why China was so backward. Ito replied to Li Hongzhang that China's poverty and backwardness were due to its inability to employ true talents. Li Hongzhang replied that China was short of talents and that the government wanted to employ good talents, but it was difficult to find them at one time. Ito said that when he was studying in the West, he had a classmate named Wu Tingfang. Wu Tingfang's knowledge was much higher than his. He asked why the Qing government had not employed this person.

Li Hongzhang heard the news and could not find the name of Wu Tingfang in his stomach. Later, after returning to China, he inquired for a long time before he knew where Wu Tingfang lived. At that time, Wu Tingfang was working as a lawyer in Hong Kong, hanging a foreign lawyer's license. He could earn one or two taels of silver a month. At that time, there were no lawyers in China. Li Hongzhang sent someone to Hong Kong to invite him to be an official in the Qing court. Wu Tingfang always refused. At that time, Li Hongzhang promised him a monthly salary of 500 taels, thinking that it was a lot. But Wu Tingfang earned more than this in Hong Kong. Finally, Li Hongzhang tried his best to donate an official title for him and sent him to be an envoy. From this point alone, we can know the darkness of the Qing court. The improper use of people led to the weakness of the country and the poverty of the people, which led to unimaginable situations. When Wu Tingfang was employed, the civilization of others had already progressed a lot and could not catch up. This is also a major reason why Japan is stronger than China.
