Mr. Liu Haisu's Reflections on Art Studies During His European Tour (Part 2)

— Ji Ping

I also opened two Chinese modern art exhibitions in Frankfurt and Heidelberg, Germany. The exhibitions were very popular with enthusiastic visitors. The news spread rapidly throughout the various states of Germany. Because of this, I feel even more strongly that international artistic exchange can showcase the greatness of Chinese art and is a very important aspect of cultural promotion abroad. One day, Li Peima, the president of the Prussian Academy of Arts, Koumeier, the curator of the Oriental Art Museum, and Dr. Schalf, the president of the Oriental Art Association, visited me. We discussed ways to organize a Chinese modern art exhibition in Berlin. Finally, the embassy officially signed an agreement with the Oriental Art Association to hold the exhibition in February 1934. It would be co-sponsored by China and Germany, with the Prussian Academy of Arts as the venue. Ten German committee members were nominated. On the Chinese side, the Minister and Vice Minister of Education, the President of the Academia Sinica, the Chinese Ambassador to Germany, and myself were initially designated as committee members to begin preparations. The remaining six members would be appointed later.

That day, Li Peima said to me, "The previous German-Japanese joint exhibition was mainly organized by the Imperial Academy of Fine Arts of Japan. If China and Germany co-organize an exhibition next time, which organization will be the main body on the Chinese side?" I said, "China will use the Academia Sinica as the main body." He asked, "The Prussian Academy of Arts has a history of forty years, and the Japanese Imperial Academy of Fine Arts has twenty-seven years. How many years has the Academia Sinica been around?" I replied, "It's only been four or five years now, but historically speaking, it has a history of over a thousand years, because national art academies were established as early as the Tang and Song dynasties." They were very familiar with the situation in China, so they were even more aware that our country's art does indeed have a long history. He also asked, "What kind of paintings will you bring to our next exhibition for us to appreciate?" I replied, "We will bring paintings that Chinese artists have created according to their own wishes and ask the artists of your country to offer guidance." The meaning was to satirize Japan for specializing in artifice and deception, exhausting themselves in creating paintings to cater to European psychology and deceive Europeans. We are unwilling to do things that way. Li said again, "That's right. The paintings that we Germans want to appreciate are the natural paintings that we want to see in our hearts, not paintings that are made solely for display in an exhibition." At this point, Li asked me to paint a light ink landscape painting. I immediately painted it based on the meaning of "qi yun sheng dong" (spiritual consonance and lifelike expression). Li looked at it carefully and commented, "The Japanese painter Koho Tsuyurei also painted a light ink landscape painting a month ago. Its power and artistic conception are far inferior. Because of this, I believe that the Chinese Modern Art Exhibition in 1934 will definitely give us satisfaction."

In the past three years, I have comprehensively reviewed the art facilities in various European countries. The scale is grand and the meaning is profound. I can't help but sigh in surprise. Looking back on the rich artistic achievements of our country for thousands of years, they far surpass those of Europe. It is most regrettable that there is a lack of strategies for preservation and development, and that they are buried under weeds, so that future scholars have no way to touch and appreciate the works of the past and find it difficult to deeply pursue further studies in modern times. All my colleagues in the art world should rise up and strive for the revival movement of art.

acting as host. Mr. Ye was a member of the Tongmenghui. During the recovery of Shanghai, he led members of the merchant corps to attack the Manufacturing Bureau. In the first year of the Republic, he escorted Mr. Sun Yat-sen to the capital to assume the position of Provisional Grand President. He did not seek fame after his success, and still sought public welfare in the locality, engaging in commerce. He was righteous and courageous, and spoke his mind frankly. You worked hard to restore Chu, emulating the loyalty of an orphan, and you were willing to smear your brain rather than submit to Qin. A man's aspirations are like spring thunder, and wealth and fame are like autumn grass. You happily return to your original clothes, and still manage your rice paddies. You don't want to spend your life idly, and you lead the business world to seek transformation. Heaven should grant him a long life, and work together to support the collapsing mansion."

Rotary Club Stories

The Pestle of Dreams (21)

— Cheng Zhanlu

"Could it be that the people here are all immortal?"

"We only live forever in the joy of the present, there is no such thing as old age or death; if there were old age and death, we would not be able to maintain our present joy, we have overthrown old age and death."

While Tao Chi was answering questions with the others at the table, another team of dancing girls came, dressed in colorful clothes, displaying their modern dance skills in front of the table; Tao Chi watched with enthusiasm, drinking several cups of modern wine, he became even more intoxicated in the joy of the present, he even more felt that the past sorrows were meddlesome, the future hopes were delusions; he only sought the present happiness, and lived forever in this long-lasting and unchanging present life.

The dancing girls finished dancing the modern dance, and then sang modern songs:

丨丨 Modern Songs 丨丨

The red sun is in the sky, the long rope is hit, tied again and again;

The past and the future are all overthrown, only the present will never change; 丨丨 the character "bian" rhymes with "bi".

The flowers are always beautiful, the days are always beautiful;

The crimson face is forever crimson, a lifetime of smiling eyes without tears 丨丨丨 read as "li".

Visit a singing girl, seek a dancing partner;

Why is there heaven? Why is there an emperor?

And with joy丨 and with games丨

Tao Chi listened to this modern song that only cared about the present happiness, his soul broke into the palace of bewilderment, he seemed to see in that palace of bewilderment, hanging many slogans, he only remembered the following three:

"Only care about the present, don't care about anything else!"

"Friends, don't ask about the past humiliations, don't think about the future difficulties, you just seek your present revelry!"

"Matter does not perish, and the present does not perish!"

Gold Market Shows Slight Reaction

The entire day was extremely volatile. Yesterday, the 22nd, the gold price suddenly experienced major changes, with storms and waves surging, advancing and retreating suddenly, with unstoppable momentum. The entire day had a difference of sixteen taels. In the morning market, initially due to the League of Nations' hesitation towards Japan, coupled with the British advocating the use of silver, the price weakened to within 710 taels. Subsequently, the exchange rate changed from loose to firm, and the posted price was reduced. The buying side on the market saw renewed excitement, suddenly turning to a high peak, and surging by 10 taels. In the afternoon market, it once exceeded the 720 tael mark, truly due to the extreme tightness of exchange drafts, and repeated contractions. This was mainly due to the buying momentum of large players. However, many parties took the opportunity to unload, and market sentiment suddenly turned weak. Therefore, it fell sharply by five or six taels. In the end, compared to the previous day, it fell by more than two taels, and the situation was chaotic, making it difficult to understand.

Opening Lower then Rising The opening of the market saw a drop of 9 taels and 4 qian to 709 taels for large bars and a drop of a quarter for silver prices. However, due to the current situation and the fact that Yuanmao, Qianchangxiang, Dadecheng, Tongtaichang, Fuchang, and others were selling, and the exchange market seemed to be easing, with banks mutually trading US dollars at 32.0625 yuan and British gold needing to be sold at 17.5 yuan, the price continued to fall. It then fell from 710 taels to 05 taels and 7 qian. Before long, Zhifeng, Yongyu, Hehong, Kangyonghengchangyong, and others came to buy in, and in just over ten minutes, it rose to 10 taels and 8 qian. HSBC initially posted British gold as before, and US dollars lengthened by 125, as it had retreated to 08 taels and 2 qian. A while later, it went from 10 taels and 2 qian to 07 taels and 7 qian, and market sentiment was calm. Around 9:50, the bank bought recent British gold at 17.5, and the forward contract settled at 17.375. Fuchang, Yifeng, Yongqian, Shixiang, Daxing, Yongyuanmao, and exchange traders were all paying in, so the price jumped 5 taels to 10 o'clock, reaching 12 taels and 8 qian. Afterwards, due to Tongtaichang, Fuchang, Dadecheng, Yifeng, Yongshunli, and others selling, US dollars needed to be sold at 32.125 yuan, which caused the market to suddenly become exhausted and immediately fell by 6 or 7 taels. At 10:30, it was only 06 taels. Afterwards, British gold and others recovered, and recent transactions were done at 17.375, and then the January contract was at 17.1875. Therefore, it showed a trend of solidity again. Yuanmao, Yonghengchangyong, Yifeng, Yongqianchangxiang, and Yuda all showed strong buying interest, and the gold price soared, exceeding 10 taels. Furthermore, British gold changed by 125 and US dollars by 25, reaching 16 taels at 11:30. However, goods traders and retail investors had already sold, and the Indian exchange rate reported "Da Er Anna", so it fell by two or three taels again. The noon close was 13 taels and 2 qian, and continued to trade to within 12 taels, and then to 13 taels. Silver Split Reaches Five Qian

Market Overview The emergency situation in the financial world is becoming increasingly urgent. The situation in the market yesterday was particularly critical. The silver split actually reached five qian. Market sentiment was very panicked. Even with the ability to support the sky, it is difficult to remedy the actual situation. As far as the eye can see, there is no hope for a turnaround within this month. However, it is necessary to forcefully suppress it, or the silver split may return to a low level, and market sentiment can be calmed. If relief is not sought immediately, the silver split will remain high for a long time, not only will there be no possibility of making loans, but the foundation itself may be worrying.

Li Split Price The price of one foreign li and one early market li has slightly recovered due to the extremely tight silver reserves. The closing price was 7 qian 2 fen 7 li and a half, which was a small 2 hao and a half less than the noon market the previous day. The afternoon market fell more sharply, at 7 qian 2 fen 6 li 6 hao and 2 hu and a half, a sudden drop of 1 li 1 hao 2 hu and a half from the early market. The two markets were a small 1 li more, mainly because the silver reserves were tight and were suppressed to be small. The "silver split" was five qian in both the early and noon markets, which was eight fen higher than the previous early market and was a new record not seen in this year. Banks posted two qian, and drawing heads with water also had more than four qian. Looking at the silver reserves as being so tight, it is not easy for the gold market to adjust.

Subsidiary Coin Market Recently, due to the extremely tight silver reserves, subsidiary coin transactions have become sluggish. The Jiangnan and Xiaoyang markets were both 6 qian 5 fen 8 li, with only 3,000 jiao of transactions made in the early market. Flour Market High in the Morning, Flat in the Afternoon

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month also showed a surge, due to the improved quotation of foreign wheat. In the foreign wheat market, there were also suspicious rumors, as if the fundamentals had already been shaken, and people's hearts could not help but be shocked. Therefore, the highest price for this month rose to 2 taels and 01 and a half cents, November to 2 taels and 03 and a half cents, December to 2 taels and 05 cents, January to 2 taels and 07 and a half cents, February to 2 taels and 08 and a half cents, and March to 2 taels and 09 and a half cents, which was 20 to 30 cents higher than the closing price of the previous day. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, it was initially stable, but then the situation turned to harmony due to the return of longs and some factory sell-offs, falling by more than 10 cents compared to the morning. As a result, this month was 5 cents better than the previous day, November was 7 and a half cents better, December was 1 and a half cents better, January was 1 and a half cents better, February was 1 and 7 and a half cents better, and March was 1 and a half cents better, it is said.

Wheat Futures Trend Higher

Yesterday, in the wheat futures market, after the opening of the market in the morning and afternoon, the market for each month showed a trend of being stable in the near term and rising in the long term. This month, due to the imminent delivery, the bulls inside and outside the industry had to close their positions, so there were few fluctuations in each round of trading. However, for the distant months, because foreign wheat was rising step by step, the general assumption was that the arrival of foreign wheat in China and the number of orders would not be as surging and unlimited as a few months ago. Because of this reason, the hearts of people inside and outside the industry naturally became excited, so the opening price also rose step by step. As a result, this month was 1 cent better than the previous day, November was 6 cents better, December was 7 cents better, January was 6 cents better, February was 4 cents better, and March was 7 cents better, it is said.

Silk, Tea, and Foreign Firms: The Silk Market Is Still Difficult to Advance

Yesterday, the silk market of foreign firms in this port was still difficult to advance. Although New York white filature had an appetite, the price of silk in the telegram was still trending flat and weak. The price of B-grade, 83% evenness, was still only 845 taels, and the factory had to lose more than 100 taels. Negotiations were still difficult to conclude. Spot sales in Lyon were still stagnant. Yesterday, only Jardine Matheson imported 20 bales of Shanghai white filature, Dachang and others imported 25 bales of Sichuan yellow filature, and Gong'an imported 10 bales of white filature, and the price remained stable, it is said.

Red and Green Tea Transactions Still Sparse

Yesterday, the tea market of foreign firms in this port still had no major progress. British firms such as Jardine Matheson and Jinlong, etc., were all holding a wait-and-see attitude because they had sent out a large number of Zhenmei telegrams and had not yet seen a reply. The whole city only bought 198 boxes of Qimen black tea and Zhenmei, Xiami, and Gongxi green tea from Dodeyuan, Shengsheng, and Fulin, etc. The market price was still extremely low, it is said.

North and South Goods: Longkou Vermicelli Fell and Rose Again

Longkou vermicelli is recently active in the market, and the market price has fallen and risen again. The initial price opened at 23 taels and 60 cents, and then rose to 23 taels and 80 cents to 24 taels. The market was even tighter yesterday, and customer goods opened another hundred bags, priced at 24 taels and a half, which was an increase of 9 taels before and after. Therefore, the market price increased accordingly, and there was no large amount of source goods that could arrive temporarily, so it is temporarily difficult to expect relaxation, it is said.

Hardware: English White Iron Plates Arrive, Selling Well and Smoothly

Since the import of thin English white iron plates from the East has stopped, the trend in this port has been unusually exciting. Therefore, in the past few days, as many as 600 to 700 boxes have been opened. However, the remaining spot goods have been searched clean, and the futures that are subsequently loaded have also been mostly sold. The price of Red Crow brand is 1 tael and 50 cents per sheet, Comet brand is 1 tael and 47 cents, and miscellaneous brands are 1 tael and 45 cents (all above are 3 feet 7 inches). The 3 feet 6 inches foreign letter brand is sold for 1 tael and 30 cents, the Triangle brand is 1 tael and 25 cents, and the miscellaneous brand is 1 tael, 20 cents and 3 cents. It was found that the Yangtze River Road is the most prosperous among the various gangs, and the business on North Henan Road is relatively less. Recently, many from Fujian and Shantou have also inquired. Although the number of orders is not large, if the exchange rate can be calculated, the transaction aspect will be prosperous, I fear.

Social News

Noteworthy Japanese Birth Rate

Four Children Born Every Minute

Asian countries today have a major problem to solve. This problem is how to solve the difficult subject of overpopulation. Great Britain, Germany, France, and the United States of America in Europe are the complete opposite, with birth rates gradually decreasing, far less than in Asia. Among the Asian countries, the increase in the Japanese population is particularly noteworthy. In recent years, the Japanese birth rate has been rising day by day, while the mortality rate is gradually decreasing. Moreover, there are many marriages and few divorces in Japan, resulting in many children. According to current statistics, four children are born every minute in Japan. Therefore, it is generally expected that in another thirty years, its national population will certainly reach 100,000,000.

Calculating at four children born every minute, the population will increase by 43,000 per month. According to the announcement by the Statistics Bureau of the Japanese Cabinet, on October 1, 1930, the total population of Japan, excluding overseas conquered territories, was 64,450,005, an increase of 4,713,183 compared to 1925, with a percentage increase of 7.9%. The increase from 1925 compared to the statistics five years earlier was 3,773,769, with a percentage increase of 6.7%.

Comparing Japan with European countries and the Americas, the situation is very different. In the last 50 years, the birth rates in Great Britain, Germany, and the United States have gradually declined, while Japan has been rising step by step. Its current population is the same as the population of England in 1870. The annual population increase rate in Japan, according to the 1930 census, is 15.30 per thousand people, while it was 13.14 ten years ago. Therefore, in thirty years, by 1960, the population of Japan could reach 100,000,000. Its population would be the same as the population of the United States in 1920. Thirty years later, the Japanese population will reach 100 million, at which time its position in terms of manpower will be third, with the United States first and Soviet Russia second. Although the future is a world of science and machinery, the words "manpower" seem to have little relevance. However, for a country like Japan, where the people are willing to endure hardship and the government is working hard, with 100 million people united in one mind, its power cannot be underestimated.

Although the Japanese government superficially encourages childbirth, many politicians secretly oppose birth control. The government takes action against merchants selling birth control devices or drugs, only allowing people with illnesses to use such things. So what methods will they ultimately use to solve this difficult problem? On the surface, they naturally say to develop domestic industries and promote overseas trade to solve the problems of overpopulation and people's livelihoods. But in reality, the Japanese archipelago cannot possibly accommodate the surging population growth. Thus, the only method is emigration. The first step is to emigrate to its conquered territories, such as Taiwan and Korea. The second step is to use violence to invade China and move Japanese people to the three northeastern provinces. The third step is simply to move Japanese people entirely to China. If we think about it with our eyes closed, in thirty years, the Japanese population will be 100 million, which is one-quarter of the current Chinese population. But does China actually have 400 million people? No, it definitely does not reach this number. In our country, natural disasters and man-made calamities have occurred throughout the years, making people unable to live. Not only is the population growth declining day by day, but even in terms of the existing number, the mortality rate is greater than in any other country on Earth, and it has long been less than 400 million. Therefore, can the increase in births and the rapid increase in population in Japan not make the Chinese people feel chilled?

The city with the largest population in Japan is Osaka, with a population of 2,453,573 people. Tokyo is second, with 2,070,913 people. These two major cities, because of the rapid increase in population, are developing incessantly towards the surrounding countryside. Tokyo, including the suburbs, has a thriving metropolitan population comparable to that of London, England, and New York, USA. There are no fewer than twenty-one cities in the suburbs of Tokyo, each with a population of 50,000 people, included in the Tokyo area. Therefore, the total population within the area is 5,408,687 people. The total population of the Osaka area is 3,540,017 people. 24% of Japan's total population resides in 109 cities, of which 28 cities have a population exceeding 1,000,000 people. In the past five years, eight new cities have been added, each with a population of 30,000 people. The six major cities with more than 500,000 residents, in addition to Osaka and Tokyo, are Nagoya, with 907,404 people, Kobe, with 787,616 people, Kyoto, with 765,142 people, and Yokohama, with 620,306 people. In addition, there are twenty-two cities, each with more than 100,000 residents.

Of the total population of Japan, 50% to 55% of the people reside in cities with a population of less than 10,000 people. In Japan, there are approximately 27,000,000 farmers, approximately 5,000,000 workers, and approximately 8,000,000 merchants. The countryside is not as rich as neighboring cities.

Social News Submission Guidelines

(1) The text is limited to news about domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, rural areas, (2) hygiene, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life.

(3) Photos are qualified if they are about seasonal events, scenery, animals, plants, people, and news photography. Photos of seasonal scenery with beautiful women are especially welcome.

Youth Zone

Voices from the Flood-Stricken Areas

— Guan Hua

A Self-Account by a Youth Suffering from Disaster

Dear compatriots, I am extremely ashamed to use such an address, given my unfortunate circumstances. But I am one who has encountered such an unfortunate environment, and in recounting my tragic suffering, perhaps the gentlemen will take pity on me. I am from Shaanxi, living in a rural village near a lake. My family owns ten mu of embanked fields, and I have both parents, an elder sister, a younger sister, and two younger brothers. Apart from me, who has received a higher primary school education, they are all illiterate. They work barefoot under the intense sunlight every day, cultivating the fields themselves. Because if we don't farm ourselves, we won't have the ability to eat and will starve to death. In normal times, our finances are already very tight. But the price of their blood and sweat, apart from providing food for our family of seven, can barely allow me to study at the higher primary school. In my situation as a poor man, it is inherently impossible to sustain my studies. But since my body is small and thin and I have no strength, I can't farm. Therefore, I have no choice but to "live one day at a time and study." In my mind, I believe that if I can receive a primary school education, I will at least be more convenient than those who don't study. I will be able to read the simplest letters and write the simplest letters. That is my only hope. At the same time, within this hope, I harbor the ambition to be self-reliant in the future. But now, this beautiful dream has been shattered. I definitely have no opportunity or hope to continue studying, and definitely no ambition to be self-reliant. That's because a torrential rain lasting dozens of days has washed away our only property—ten mu of fields—turning them into a vast ocean. I can't even distinguish where the shadows of our fields are. So, what can we do? Beg? That won't have any results, because there are too many people begging now. There are beggars on the east side and beggars on the west side. People may doubt that I am not really begging and may think that I am hanging a "sign" of begging and wearing a "mask" of pleading. For this reason, I have decided not to beg. But how can we live? This question is pressing me tightly. So, my family and I decided to move to a place without floods. In our ideal, we also dreamed that we would find a philanthropist who would help us and give us the chance to not die temporarily. At the same time, we hoped that in our struggle with fate, we might find a position that would maintain the minimum standard of living, making our hopes brighter and making us feel some of the interest of life and the spirit of struggle. Therefore, in the climate of wind and rain, we walked one step at a time to a relatively high village more than five li away from us—a village that has not suffered much flooding. Dear compatriots, five li is such a short journey. In normal times, we could reach our destination in one hour. But in these days of hunger and cold, it's really two steps for every one step. We walked for two hours before discovering our New World—our destination. When we arrived there, we began to ask the people in that relatively fortunate village. But when they saw us in such a dilapidated state, they not only didn't give us any comfort or inquiries, they even turned their heads away from us and walked to the other side with a sneer. This was a major blow to us who were in "dire straits at dusk." This major blow made us tremble, as if we had walked into a mountain valley where wolves and tigers gathered, with a big river in front and pursuing soldiers behind us. We couldn't help but cry loudly, cursing our bleak fate. How miserable we cried! We cried for an hour, but still didn't see the shadow of anyone. Humans are truly cruel animals. They only know how to take care of their own happiness. They only care about eating comfortably, living comfortably, and using things comfortably. How can they care about their compatriots? How can they know that besides their own parents, wives, and children, there are other human beings? How can they know the greatness of giving sympathy? How can they know the true painful life of the people in the flood-stricken areas, a life that cannot be endured? How can they know that people as unfortunate as us have drifted to their village? How can they hear our cries of blood and tears? We were thinking that we had come to the gates of hell. Having suffered so much contempt and so much hunger, it would be better to die cleanly than to stand here crying like this. We wouldn't have to run this five li journey step by step. Why would we pour out our passionate cries in such a village? Why would I bring my parents, sisters, and brothers to suffer? If they died at home, waiting for the water to overwhelm them, wouldn't that be five li less of walking? Wouldn't that reduce the contempt of people? I was thinking, hating, and repenting, when suddenly, unexpectedly, an old man near sixty years old stood in front of us. He comforted us and asked us the reason for our crying. When he saw that our throats were hoarse from crying, he gave us a few cups of tea and a few bowls of rice. He tried his best to satisfy our hunger. After we finished eating the rice and tea, he invited us to live in his home. Needless to say, we were of course extremely grateful. He introduced his wife and son to us, and they all talked to us very happily. We told them in detail about our suffering, and they shed tears of sympathy, pity, and comfort. We lived quietly in the old man's house, and life was of course relatively quiet. But thinking about the suffering of those who continue to suffer from the flood, I can't help but shed tears. We have been living in that old man's house for more than half a month. More than half a month is of course not a long period, but when I think about everything in the quiet night, thinking about their great burden for us, wouldn't that add an economic "cross" to their simple family? Wouldn't that make them unable to express their suffering? Wouldn't that create a phenomenon where we feel uneasy while eating? Wouldn't that make us think that we have no ability to repay them? Wouldn't that be a major annoyance in our hearts? How can we live in peace? How can we live in peace with such a heart? Dear compatriots, how can we live in peace? But I have now decided. I have decided to have my parents, sisters, and brothers taken care of by them, having them do some work for the old man's family. I have decided not to live there any longer. I want to carve out a path from my bad environment, be proactive, advance, and struggle. Then I will be worthy of being called an educated youth. Then I will be a part of the responsibility of undertaking the future of our nation. Then I will walk on the path of light. Dear compatriots, I, who have just experienced the suffering of the flood, and at the same time lack the cultivation of knowledge and the experience of society, am very much in need of your timely guidance. Dear compatriots,
